Statistics on Drug Trafficking Cases Cracked in the Past Nine Months 22

U.S. Representative Reports at the Opium Advisory Committee

Hu Shize Asks to Pay Attention to China's Smoke Prohibition Situation

[Geneva] At today's meeting of the Opium Advisory Committee, U.S. representative Fuller presented a report with statistics on private drug smuggling cases cracked in the first nine months of this year. During those nine months, cases of private smuggling of raw opium were cracked in China, the United States, Hong Kong, Macau, the Dutch East Indies, Siam, Iraq, Egypt, Turkey, France, England, the Netherlands, and other countries. The largest case of private drug smuggling was cracked in New York on June 16, with 183 kilograms of drugs seized. The batch of drugs was transported from Marseille by a Norwegian wheel, passing through Spain and Portugal to the United States. The next largest case was cracked in Marseille on May 8, with 52 kilograms of raw opium seized. This opium was transported from the Far East, Turkey, Egypt, and other places. In addition, more than 11 and a half kilograms of raw opium were cracked in Rotterdam on September 18. The sources of the cracked cases in Europe and the United States have not been determined. Those cracked in the Far East included opium from Turkey, Persia, and China. In addition, there were those coming from Siberia. The Persian opium cracked in the Far East had special marks and similar marks. Most of the private drug trafficking marks were used. Opium was also cracked twice in Trinidad, Spain. According to the smugglers, the opium was smuggled from British India to Europe. The smuggling of cooked opium was mostly in Hong Kong, the Dutch East Indies, Siam, the Philippines, and the United States. It was also cracked in England, the Netherlands, and New Zealand. Most of the seals and marks were Chinese, and it seems that they were loaded and exported from the coastal ports of China. The largest amount of morphine cracked was in the Far East and the United States. There were only two cases in Poland and three in Turkey in Europe. The United States cracked 19 cases, with a total of 6 kilograms of morphine. China had 7 cases, Hong Kong had 1 case, and Siam had the most with 94 cases. In the Far East and the United States, there have been constant cracking of morphine manufacturing organizations. Heroin smuggling cases in the nine months included one case each in the United States, Canada, and Hong Kong, and eight cases in China. One of the cases cracked in Hong Kong had 128 kilograms. The investigation is still in progress. It is said that the heroin in Hong Kong was transported from Guangzhou and it is believed that it was manufactured in South China. However, another report stated that it was manufactured in Japan. There were also reports of crackdowns in Canada, the United States, the Philippines, China, the South Seas Islands, India, Austria, France, Italy, Greece, Poland, and Uruguay. A large amount of cocaine, up to 21 kilograms, was cracked in Shanghai. It is said that the drugs were found on a Japanese ship and were manufactured in Japan. Fuller's report has been passed by the committee. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 23rd)

[London] Hu Shize, the Chinese envoy to Switzerland, delivered an article to the League of Nations' Opium Committee today, asking it to pay attention to the new laws and regulations recently implemented in China to ban the buying and selling of opium. Hu said that the problem is more serious in China because the regulations governing the buying and selling of opium are more strictly enforced in China than in the West, and the events in the Far East have prevented China from giving the matter all the necessary attention. This is also the reason why the opium problem is becoming more serious. The anti-drug movement in China cannot be limited to unilateral actions by China. China needs the cooperation of the powers in China that have concessions and settlements, because foreigners in the concessions and settlements who sell drugs are punished too lightly. (Reuters dispatch on the 22nd)

Officer of the Hai Rui Warship Executed for Private Drug Trafficking 23

[Guangzhou] The Guangdong Naval Headquarters announced today that Li Tang (transliteration), an officer of the Hai Rui warship, has been executed for private opium trafficking in accordance with the recently passed anti-drug regulations implemented by the Southwest Political Affairs Council. As for the legal disposition of the administrative agency to order the relocation of graves for public interest, the owner of the grave cannot resist it. Current Commentary

The Future of Indian Self-Government 31

— Ting

India, known as an ancient civilization of the world, has been under the control of the British for more than 300 years. Even the history of its direct rule by the British government is nearly 80 years. The British regard India as nothing more than a private possession. However, due to the vigorous self-determination movement in recent years, they have not hesitated to make false concessions and gradually changed from a high-pressure policy to a policy of appeasement. However, their desire to permanently control it has never changed.

What the Indian people demand is independence and autonomy, or at least the rights that a self-governing colony should enjoy. However, the British are only willing to discuss the revision of the current Indian constitution, formally replacing centralization with a federal system. Nothing else is their concern. Since 1930, the British have convened round table conferences on constitutional issues three times. Their purpose is nothing more than to use the beautiful name of "self-government" to eliminate the proposal of "complete independence" passed by the Indian National Congress in Lahore in 1919.

After the Third Round Table Conference, the British government issued a White Paper describing the proposals for revising the Indian Constitution. The main points were that the executive power of the Indian Federation would be in the hands of the Governor-General, who would restrain and manage the affairs of the ministries of national defense, foreign affairs, and religion. The Legislative Council may not pass any laws that would restrict or discriminate against the exercise of certain franchised rights by British or British companies. The true face of the British government was even more exposed at this point. It is appropriate that there were widespread repercussions and proposals for revision. Now, looking at the recently published report on Indian constitutional reform, the power of the Governor-General is still very extensive, and the special status of the British in India is explicitly guaranteed. With such regulations, not only is the reality of complete autonomy far away, but it is also a dream to be equal to self-governing colonies such as Canada. It is in order for the Indians to riot and resist.

However, we must silently observe the internal affairs of India and realize that the Indians themselves also have their own faults. The independence movement is to seek political freedom and national liberation, and the spirit of political democracy must be based on the spirit of social democracy. However, the intensity of religious and ethnic conflicts in India and the depth of class concepts are rare in the world. How can the British not take advantage of this weakness to manipulate them in the middle, so that 300 million Indians will never be free. For example, the Indian National Congress was originally a tool for all Indians to seek the benefits of independence. However, the most powerful Hindus and Muslims in the Indian nation have different dreams in the same bed and have always adhered to their prejudices and refused to cooperate sincerely. As a result, the National Congress, which bears a major mission, cannot exert its due power. For so many years, although important domestic leaders such as Gandhi and Madam Nehru have been running around mediating and repeatedly persuading, the results have been minimal, which is regrettable.

Now, let us take a step back and say that the newly published constitutional outline has exhausted the ability of fairness and generosity. However, the infighting between the Hindu and Muslim religions will still make the election of key members of the whole case have no satisfactory solution. Looking at past experience, the claims of the Hindu and Muslim religions will immediately conflict as soon as the election is mentioned. The reason is that the number of Hindus is more than 240 million, accounting for about three-quarters of the total population. The number of Muslims is more than 68 million, accounting for about one-fifth of the total population. The Hindus rely on their large number of people and advocate that the production of members should be elected by the "joint election system," that is, all ethnic voters are gathered in one place, and those with the most votes are elected. Muslims advocate the "separate election system," that is, each ethnic group separately elects a certain number of members to organize the parliament. (However, in the two provinces of Bengal and Punjab, where the number of this religion is uniquely large, they also advocate joint elections.) In addition, they also require that any proposal in the legislature must be approved and implemented by two-thirds of all Muslim representatives, otherwise it will be completely invalid. Both sides insist on their own opinions and refuse to give in. Now it is heard that the constitutional report stipulates that each minority has seats in the parliament of the federation and provinces. However, whether it can be smoothly allocated in fact is still a big question. If this is not resolved, any constitutional reform cannot be discussed. If the British have the sincerity to help India's self-government, why not add to it?

About a month ago, the All-India Congress met in Mumbai. The chairman severely criticized the British White Paper policy in his opening remarks. He concluded by saying, "We are fighting barehanded with the weapons of morality against a government equipped with the latest destructive machinery to fight for justice. God will bless us." His words are extremely painful. However, while Indians hope for God's blessing, we especially hope that Indians can help themselves.

Hungary Should Be Held Responsible for the Marseille Incident and Endangers Peace 32

Southern Kingdom Officially Accuses League of Nations

Request to Include in Next Agenda for Discussion

[Geneva] The Yugoslav government's application to the League of Nations regarding the issue of political responsibility for the assassination in Marseille has been submitted by the country's Foreign Minister, Yevtic, to the Secretariat of the League of Nations. The application states that the Marseille assassination is of great importance and enough to disrupt relations between the Southern Kingdom and Hungary, because some terrorists are sheltered by Hungary and receive assistance from certain government offices. The application then states that the Southern Kingdom has directly negotiated with Hungary regarding the activities of terrorist parties, and a compromise was reached in the Southern Kingdom's capital in July of this year. Hungary agreed to prohibit them, but according to recent investigations, terrorist parties are still sheltered by Hungary. Therefore, the murder of King Alexander and French Foreign Minister Barthou was committed by these people, and the prior arrangements were also carried out in Hungary. Furthermore, an investigation revealed that some of the accomplices in the Marseille case had previously committed crimes and were accused by Yugoslavia to Hungary. According to their confessions, it is evident that they were not only sheltered by Hungary, but also lived in groups within Hungary, until just before the Marseille incident occurred. Yugoslavia also intends to submit a number of documents as proof of the events listed in the application. The Southern Kingdom government requests that this case be included in the agenda of the League of Nations so that it can be discussed at the next Executive Council meeting. (According to reports, in mid-May of this year, the Hungarian government submitted an application to the League of Nations regarding an incident that occurred on the Hungarian-Southern border. After the Southern Kingdom also submitted a memorandum, the Executive Council intended to discuss the matter, but the two countries, South and Hungary, suddenly had the intention of direct negotiations, so it was abandoned. The compromise reached in the Southern Kingdom's capital in July mentioned in this telegram is probably the result of direct negotiations between the two countries.) (Havas News Agency, 22nd)

Romania and Czechoslovakia Send Documents to the League of Nations

Voicing Support for Southern Kingdom

[Geneva] After the government of the Southern Kingdom submitted its application to the League of Nations regarding political responsibility for the Marseille assassination, the governments of Czechoslovakia and Romania also sent official documents to the League of Nations separately. Their contents were the same, stating briefly that the two governments believe that the political responsibility for the Marseille case is sufficient to disrupt the relations between the countries and Hungary, so the two governments express their sympathy for the application submitted by the Southern Kingdom to the League of Nations. (Havas News Agency, 22nd)

Clearly Political Purpose

Hungary Expresses Protest

Budapest - Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös issued a statement to the semi-official news agency, expressing a serious protest against the actions of the Yugoslav government, and explaining in detail the views of his government on this issue, saying that this behavior is detrimental to the peace of Europe. The Hungarian Prime Minister claimed that the Hungarian government was not surprised by the documents in this Marseille incident, but regarded it merely as a further step in newspaper propaganda. This propaganda has been commonplace for several months, with the aim of damaging Hungary's position. However, the tone of this document is the same as what is published in the newspapers, which is strange. The Hungarian government will ask the world to pay attention to the political role of the Yugoslav documents. Hungary has been established for nearly a thousand years, and its history has never condoned such political assassinations. Therefore, in the capacity of a representative of Hungary, it lodges a serious protest against the Yugoslav documents and denies all fabricated accusations. (National News Agency, 23rd)

Hungarian Representative to the League of Nations, Adachi, immediately responded to this challenge, stating that he very much wanted to have the opportunity to debate the Marseille incident in the League of Nations Executive Council. Adachi also said, "I am absolutely opposed to this kind of strategy. I think this is no different from international terrorism." The so-called strategy refers to the accusation of the Southern Kingdom. (National News Agency, 22nd)

Great Shock in Geneva

France Faces Dilemma

[Geneva] According to political observers, the application from the Southern Kingdom to the League of Nations, which strongly accuses Hungary, has caused quite a stir here. France and the Little Entente countries also find themselves in a dilemma, because a few days ago, French Foreign Minister Laval had consulted with representatives of the Little Entente repeatedly, but unexpectedly, the result was like this. All parties speculate that the Southern Kingdom will submit concrete evidence to support its application. According to the Southern Kingdom, these documents will soon be made public to prove that it is not a false accusation. Although the application is only against Hungary, under the observation of all parties, it will further cause disputes between the Southern Kingdom and Italy. In this case, the recent compromise movement between Italy, France, and the Little Entente countries will inevitably be hit. In particular, the application from the Southern Kingdom will not be submitted to the Executive Council of the League of Nations for discussion until January next year. (National News Agency, 23rd)

The Content is Divided into Four Items

Avoid Using Written Clauses

Austrian and Hungarian Prime Ministers Scheduled to Meet

According to these people, the Austrian-Italian military agreement was agreed upon orally by the two Prime Ministers without using written clauses. Convention on Arms Control 34

Three Points for Britain to Consider

[London] Foreign Secretary Simon made a speech in the House of Commons today, saying that regarding the issue of state monopoly on arms manufacturing, preparations are underway to conduct an investigation. Simon said that regarding this matter, the government's intentions in Geneva are roughly three-fold: (1) Effective supervision of arms, and a ban on state subsidies to arms merchants and the granting of loans to facilitate exports; (2) All countries should apply licensing methods to arms manufacturing for the purpose of supervision; (3) The state of arms manufacturing must be made public, but should not hinder national security. Simon concluded that regarding the state monopoly on arms sales, it seemed to be a partial concession to the opposition Liberal Party and Labour Party. He said, "The government is of course opposed to investigating the situation of arms sales and lightly listening to all kinds of rumors, so as to involve foreign affairs, but if we seriously study the issue of state monopoly on arms sales in terms of national security, then the situation is completely different." Simon then explained what procedures should be adopted if such an investigation is conducted. (Havas News Agency, 22nd)

Japanese Cabinet Reaches Agreement on Annual Budget 39

The Total Amount Reaches 2.3 Billion Yuan, with Military Expenses Accounting for Half

3 Million Yuan More Than This Year's Budget

Military Adds 57.9 Million Yuan

[Tokyo] The first approved draft of the general budget for next year is 2.043 billion yen, plus the total amount of additional budgets approved, totaling 98 million yen, and 65 million yen for disaster budgets, etc., totaling 2.206 billion yen. There will be an increase of 5-6 million yen, so the budget for next year will actually reach an unprecedented amount, and the total amount of public bonds issued will be about 700 million yen. (Japan United News Agency, 23rd)

[Tokyo] The total number of the budget has now reached 2.206 billion yen, and the national defense budget reaches 1.021 billion yen, (including the navy's 530 million yen), accounting for 48% of the total budget. (Japan United News Agency, 23rd)

[Tokyo] The Japanese government's budget for the Showa 10th year was facing reefs due to the national defense budget issue, and it could not be resolved for a long time. However, the cabinet meeting on the 22nd, which lasted until 3:00 am this morning, took a sudden turn for the worse, and it was decided to approve an additional 57.9 million yen for the military budget. The army and navy were divided in half, each receiving 27 million yen, and the rest was for interest payments on public bonds. The source of funds for the above budget is as follows: an additional 40 million yen in public bonds, 2.4 million yen in special accounting for communications from the Ministry of Communications, 14.5 million yen in special accounting from the Ministry of Railways, and 960,000 yen in special accounting from the Taiwan Governor-General's Office, totaling approximately 57.9 million yen. The entire budget for the army and navy is as follows (in units of 1,000 yen):

Army Budget

Total number of first decision 451,000

First resurrection approved 13,000

Second resurrection approved 27,000

Total 491,000

Navy Budget

Basic budget 395,000

Total number of first decision 95,000

First resurrection approved 13,000

Second resurrection approved 27,000

Total 530,000

Finance Minister Fujii considered the 40 million yen of resurrection requests from various provinces to be the maximum amount approved by the Ministry of Finance, and stubbornly defended his fiscal policy. Therefore, the third budget cabinet meeting on the 22nd was indeed in turmoil, and it was not resolved until dawn the next day, creating a new precedent in financial history. The initial budget determined by the Ministry of Finance was 2.042 billion yen, the number of approvals for the first resurrection request was 40 million yen, and the resurrection budget decided at dawn on the 23rd was 43 million yen, plus the 60 million yen budget for disaster relief in the tenth year, totaling 2.185 billion yen, an increase of 3 million yen compared to this year's budget. Finance Minister Fujii merged the disaster budgets of various places with the general budget and the general budget for review. Although the military strongly demanded resurrection, he only approved 80 million yen, and reduced the number of public bonds issued from 810 million yen to 750 million yen. From a political standpoint, Finance Minister Fujii's budget compilation policy was a great success (Japan United News Agency, 22nd).

There are Two Ways to Break the Stalemate of the Naval Conference 40

Allow Japan to Gradually Achieve Equality

Simon Believes it is More Promising

British and American Consultation on Actions Against Japan

[London] British Foreign Secretary Simon made a statement in the House of Commons today, completely denying the claim that the naval talks between Britain, the United States, and Japan have been decided. This means that there are still three ways to break the stalemate.

(1) Recover the ideal of allowing Japan to gradually achieve equality over a number of years in a certain way.

(2) Finally reach the equality of "4.4.4.", then the British and American navies must reduce matters.

(3) Japan accepts only discussions on qualitative restrictions.

The first way seems to be the most promising, because there are reasons to believe that Japan may clearly help to seek this solution. The second way is probably not favored by Britain and the United States, and the third way is also difficult to achieve, because refusing to discuss quantitative restrictions and only qualitative restrictions is one of the fundamental points of the Japanese plan. It is heard that the outside world has spread the rumor that Japan has officially acknowledged that Britain has the right to place a larger fleet than Japan, but does not acknowledge that the United States has this right. This is not accurate. Japan has requested a common higher limit for all countries, and Britain is also included in this.

Simon told the House of Commons today that the naval talks are still in progress, and it is unwise to announce the details at this time, but he can show its broad outlines.

Japan opposes the current rate In the current talks, Japan has made some suggestions, the purpose of which is to agree on a system in which each country can build ships to a common higher limit, that is, to reach its due total tonnage. The content of Japan's suggestions and the methods of reconciling differences raised by all parties cannot be reported in detail at this time.

Competition Leads to Disasters Simon continued, "The British government regards the breakdown of the naval restriction system as a disaster for everyone, not only for the countries that are currently meeting, but also for the whole world. If countries resume the arms race, the financial and political disasters will be obvious and there is no need to elaborate. The representatives of the British government do not have the will to break up the talks at all. If there is a glimmer of hope and a way to reconcile differences can be found, they intend to conduct the talks in a very friendly spirit.

Interpreting Equality The equality of security is an indisputable right that everyone should have, but this does not mean that the size of the fleets of all countries should be exactly the same. This depends on the responsibility in each event and the nature of everything else. The main purpose of our current discussion is to do our best to agree on a basis that can be used to obtain understanding without endangering the meaning of anyone's security. If we can roughly achieve this point, then we feel that there is a way to go for next year's conference. Of course, this will still depend on the opinions of the signatory countries such as France and Italy.

Notify France and Italy at Any Time Simon concluded that the United Kingdom has always been in close and friendly contact with other parties, and all developments in the naval talks are notified to the representatives of France and Italy at any time. (Reuters News Agency, 22nd)

Three British-American Consultations 41

Careful Consideration of Security and Equality

The Talks Did Not Involve Political Scope

[London] The third British-American consultation, which is the preparatory consultation for the current major crisis, seeks to discover any way out, and focuses on political diplomacy, began at 10:15 am on the 23rd in the British House of Commons. The British side was attended by British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon, and the American side was attended by Representative Davis and Councilor Atherton. (Japan United News Agency, 23rd)

[London] After the British and American naval representatives met this morning, they firmly decided to continue exploring the issues. Both sides' representatives believed that there was no reason to abandon the hope of a final compromise. The British representative informed the American representative of the situation of the meeting between Foreign Secretary Simon and Japanese Ambassador Matsudaira earlier this week. The British and American delegations both acknowledged that Japan is now only concerned with the common maximum limit, and everyone believes that the exploration of both sides will focus on why Japan needs this, and to what extent Britain and the United States can accommodate this request. (Reuters News Agency, 23rd)

[London] Foreign Secretary Simon's claim that all countries are equal in security seems to have been agreed to by the American naval representatives. British and American representatives are now considering asking Japan some new questions based on the equality of security. British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon met with American Chief Representative Davis and American Embassy Counselor Atherton in the Prime Minister's office in the House of Commons this morning for two hours. After the talks, according to people from the American delegation, MacDonald and Simon informed Davis of the details of Simon's meeting with Japanese Ambassador Matsudaira. Then, British and American representatives exchanged views for a long time. It is reported that the result was very satisfactory, and it has been decided to continue to consider the possibility of reaching an understanding. However, no "agreement" has been reached between Britain and the United States, and the establishment of a "joint front" has not become an issue. It is also heard that the talks between British and American representatives this morning have not gone beyond the political scope of the naval issue and involved the technical scope. However, the current procedures for the naval talks have been raised for consideration. The above is the news obtained from the American delegation. Apart from this, it is generally believed that the opinions of the two main points between Britain and the United States seem to be consistent. First, the American representative stated that he fully agreed with Foreign Secretary Simon's explanation of security equality in the House of Commons yesterday. Second, the British and American delegations seemed to have considered asking Japan, based on the equality of security, the reason why it made the naval request, which was the change in the situation in the Far East after the signing of the Washington Treaty. However, what kind of changes have taken place in the situation in the Far East that are sufficient to increase the strength of the British and American navies? Or the reason for the increase in the strength of the Japanese navy? After the British and American representatives held talks this morning, Davis went to the countryside with Stanley, the Chief of Naval Operations of the American representative, to play golf. He will return to London around this evening. (Havas News Agency, 23rd)

Using Tactics, Japan Attempts to Divide Britain and the United States 42

Rumors of a British-Japanese Non-Aggression Treaty

As a Means of Threatening the United States

[London] The naval delegations of Britain and the United States will hold a meeting tomorrow. American people seem to fear that someone will use means to attribute the responsibility for the failure of the initial naval talks to the United States. Moreover, the American representative's mentality of maintaining the main principles seems to be more determined than before. Although the Washington government recently sent supplementary instructions to its representatives, the American government is still fundamentally opposed to the revision of the current treaty. It is rumored tonight that in order to subdue the United States, Britain and Japan may conclude a British-Japanese non-aggression treaty as the first stage of British-Japanese rapprochement, thinking to threaten the United States with this. However, Britain has always faithfully adhered to the promise of the Washington Nine-Power Treaty, and the firm intentions of its various autonomous territories and most of British public opinion, as well as the desire to preserve British-American relations, make the claim of British-Japanese rapprochement temporarily untrustworthy. (Havas News Agency, 22nd)

[Tokyo] It is heard that Britain and the United States have always intended to propose the political issues of the Far East in the London Naval Conference for discussion. However, until recently, the naval conference was in fact unable to break away from a state of stagnation, and the claim of revising the Nine-Power and Four-Power Treaties was rampant in Britain and the United States. At this juncture, the news that Ambassador Matsudaira met with Foreign Secretary Simon on the 19th and 21st to discuss political issues suddenly gave a great impetus to all sides. According to the news from all sides, the political issues discussed by Matsudaira and Simon seemed to be a new Pacific Locarno Treaty. According to the Japanese government's opinion, if this new treaty can promote the good relations between Britain, Japan, and the United States, and can achieve non-war work, and establish peace between the three countries in any form, then Japan will not hesitate to consider this issue. The conclusion of this treaty is not the renewal of the Nine-Power Treaty or the Four-Power Treaty, and it is completely separate from these two treaties and the naval conference. On the new foundation of ensuring peace in the Pacific, the so-called Pacific Locarno Treaty will be newly concluded. However, if this treaty is used as an exchange condition for determining Japan's military strength, Japan will absolutely oppose it. (Japan United News Agency, 23rd)

Second Step: The "Compromise Proposal" in the British Naval Talks 43

[London] As the British government's attempt to negotiate a preliminary naval agreement has failed, it is now proposing the following three countermeasures as a second step:

(1) Qualitative Limitations

(2) Limitations on Pacific Defenses

(3) Notification of Shipbuilding Plans

These three points form the basis of the so-called "Compromise Proposal." It is reported that this proposal has already been presented to the American representative, and it will soon be formally presented to the Japanese delegation. The Japanese delegation is currently carefully considering this proposal, and its general intentions are as follows: (1) Absolutely disagree with the qualitative limitations proposal; (2) Have no objection to the continuation of limitations on Pacific defenses; (3) Shipbuilding notification is not a major issue and does not require special attention.

Moreover, the above items are all matters outside of the scope of instructions, so there is no need to request instructions from the home government. On the other hand, the American government has expressed absolute opposition to the separate continuation of limitations on Pacific defenses. Therefore, the attitudes of the Japanese and American delegations towards this Compromise Proposal are diametrically opposed. (22nd United Press dispatch)

Naval Equality Should Start with Reductions 44

Japanese Ambassador to the U.S. advocates a 2:2:2 Ratio

Asia's Mainland Would Inevitably Be at Japan's Mercy

U.S. Authorities Indicate This is Unacceptable

[Washington] The Japanese government's statement that it agrees that naval equality should start with arms reduction was first heard today. The Japanese Embassy in Washington explained that, according to a statement by Ambassador Saitō published in the Christian Science Monitor, Japan advocates that all countries maintain smaller navies. Japan does not insist on the "5:5:3" or "4:4:4" naval ratio between the United States, Britain, and Japan, but is willing to accept a ratio of "3:3:3" or "2:2:2." Ambassador Saitō solemnly denied that he had told the Christian Science Monitor that domestic Japanese opinions on naval issues were divided, or that army and navy leaders now want to pressure the Prime Minister to expand armaments. He only hopes to avoid unnecessary naval competition. (22nd Guomin News Agency dispatch)

[Washington] According to private expressions from U.S. authorities today, the U.S. government still cannot accept Ambassador Saitō's proposal of a 2:2:2 naval ratio. With such reductions in naval power, it would only be sufficient for use as a maritime police force, and the Asian mainland would inevitably be entirely at the mercy of Japan. Furthermore, this approach would result in Britain and the United States dismantling far more warships than Japan. In addition, the State Department stated that unless the Open Door Policy is changed, the United States will consistently oppose any movement for large-scale naval reduction. (22nd Guomin News Agency dispatch)

Japan Indicates No Change in Original Policy 45

Seeking to Reach a Common Maximum

Washington Treaty Should Be Fundamentally Abolished

[London] After another meeting between Foreign Minister Simon and Japanese Ambassador to Britain Matsudaira yesterday afternoon, a British spokesperson said that "the pessimistic mood has decreased compared to before." Today, Japanese representative Rear Admiral Yamamoto specifically issued a statement to this newspaper's reporter to correct this, saying that although Ambassador Matsudaira's conversation with Foreign Minister Simon was extremely cordial, it did not indicate a change in Japan's attitude. The Japanese representatives are still determined to continue to make sincere efforts to abolish the Washington Naval Treaty and replace it with a more appropriate treaty. In my opinion, the Washington Treaty should be fundamentally abolished, and it is inappropriate to consider retaining any of its clauses. The current priority should be to establish a foundation for worldwide compromise, and not to limit it to the five countries (Britain, the United States, Japan, France, and Italy) that signed the Washington Treaty, or the three countries (Britain, the United States, and Japan) that signed the London Treaty. Yamamoto also said that if a certain country believes that it is in the international interest to extend the qualitative limitations of the Washington Naval Treaty, then I believe that Japan would be happy to agree. (22nd Havas News Agency dispatch)

[London] The Japanese delegation to the naval talks recently issued the following declaration: "Recently, newspaper reports about the naval talks have varied. Some say that Japan has acknowledged that Britain's naval power can be stronger than that of the United States and Japan, while others say that Japan has suggested that the naval power of Britain, the United States, and Japan should have a ratio of 5:4:4. All these rumors are not accurate and have no basis. Japan has repeatedly and clearly announced to the world that in the naval talks, it is determined to make its utmost efforts to reach a reasonable agreement based on the principle of a 'common maximum.'" (23rd Havas News Agency dispatch)

Saitō Denies Writing Article for American Newspaper 46

Said to be a Journalist's Summary of His Remarks

Reviewed and Signed by Saitō Himself

[Tokyo] Former Prime Minister Count Saitō today denied writing an article for the American Christian Science Monitor regarding the naval conference, saying that he has not seen a reporter from that newspaper in recent months, nor has he written an article for the newspaper. However, in early August he read an article by a certain journalist, but it had nothing to do with arms reduction. According to the Christian Science Monitor, Saitō's remarks included that the London Naval Conference must succeed for the sake of world peace, and that anyone with correct thinking should know that bankrupting naval competition cannot achieve anything. Mr. Hersch, who compiled the article, said that the article disclosed by the Science Monitor a few days ago was written in August and was the result of several meetings with Saitō. The article summarized his views on the future of the navy. Saitō reviewed it, made corrections, and signed it. (23rd Reuters News Agency dispatch)

[Washington] The Christian Science Weekly recently published an article that it claimed contained statements by former Japanese Prime Minister Saitō. The Japanese Ambassador to the United States, Saitō, has partially denied this article. The Ambassador formally stated that former Prime Minister Saitō had met with a journalist in August 1934 and made remarks, but the article published by the Christian Science Weekly is not something that the former Prime Minister can acknowledge, and he has not even seen it. Most of the content of the article published by the Christian Science Weekly is true, and Ambassador Saitō does not deny it. However, he solemnly denies the sections criticizing Japanese political parties, stating that Japanese public opinion on naval issues is divided, and that Japanese extremists are carrying out their conspiracies, intending to build the world's strongest navy. He said that the former Prime Minister did not make such statements. The Japanese Ambassador took the opportunity to declare that Japan has not sought to establish a 5:4:4 ratio between the navies of Britain, the United States, and Japan. The only basis that Japan can accept is a 3:3:3 ratio. (22nd Havas News Agency dispatch)

Ministry of Finance Approves Two Measures for Investigating and Suppressing Refined Salt 55

[Nanjing] The Ministry of Finance replied to refined salt merchants, stating that the refined salt trade is limited to commercial ports throughout the country, as stipulated in the General Rules for Refined Salt. The locations of sales and tax payment methods will all be handled in accordance with established regulations and there will be no changes. Regarding the Shandong judgment case cited in the petition, the Salt Bureau believes that due to the different situations in each region, it is not appropriate to generalize the Shandong trial's judgment case to the entire country. An order has been issued to the Shandong Transportation Commissioner regarding this matter, and it should not be used as a basis for nationwide sales. As for the tax police's investigation and suppression of refined salt, it should be carried out when there are violations of the General Rules for Refined Salt. If the tax police interfere excessively, they should be stopped. The Ministry has now approved two measures: (1) Tax police, regardless of location, may not directly search people's homes for refined salt, nor do they need to monitor salt sales in front of salt stores. This applies when there are reports of refined salt being sold for profit in the interior; (2) If the purchase of refined salt in the original special case areas does not exceed the specified quantity, it should be released upon investigation en route. If other circumstances are found, it should be handled in accordance with the regulations. It is expected that the refined salt merchants will be notified to strictly abide by the specified sales scope in order to emphasize the salt law. (23rd special dispatch)

American Silver: The Menteith silver market is sluggish, and prices have fallen slightly.

Ms. Yang Jianxia Challenges Russian Oreste to a Martial Arts Match 86

Oreste Makes Exaggerated Propaganda in Beiping

Beiping Martial Arts Circles Rise Up in Anger to Fight for National Honor

Ms. Yang is the Daughter of a Xingyiquan Instructor

Speaks Freely About Internal and External Skills and the Characteristics of National Martial Arts

Beiping Correspondence: The social atmosphere in Beiping's lower and middle classes is characterized by both aristocratic, feudal, and class superstitions, and inherited habits of chivalry and generosity. In the late Qing Dynasty, before the era of police, local bullies roamed the streets, and women often dared not travel alone. The final degenerate form of this in Tianjin is called "Hunhun," while in Beijing it is called "Bashijiang" or "Wushujia" (martial artists). Although they do not know what formal chivalry looks like, they all have lessons from novels like "Seven Heroes and Five Gallants" or "The Cases of Peng Gong and Shi Gong" in their minds. They value loyalty and friendship, which are their strengths, but they also have a propensity for bravery, fighting, and violating the law with force, which is their weakness. For this reason, since the Republic of China, martial artists from other provinces and wandering performers, whenever they want to come to Beiping to perform or show off, must first pay respects in advance and hold a grand banquet for famous Beijing martial artists. Even the pillars of society, semi-gentry and semi-hooligans, high-level rogues, must be listed and invited to support the occasion, otherwise antipathy will arise, and they will use every means to make them fail on the spot and leave in disgrace. This is because Beiping and Hebei Province are indeed rich in martial arts talent, with fathers and sons, teachers and disciples, passing down secret oral formulas. Whether in theory or practice, they are not comparable to those who lack a family tradition or teacher. It is very easy for a large number of "insiders" and experts to concentrate and nitpick on one person. The social customs of Beiping, inherited from history, have long possessed such xenophobic roots, and coupled with the recent rise of patriotic thought and nationalism, they view it as even more developed. If a foreigner or someone from a different region comes to Beiping to perform, the Beiping society will not allow them to succeed, and this is naturally expected. This time, the Russian, Makarov, came to Beiping from Tianjin to sell martial arts. He neither paid respects in advance nor made extensive advertisements, claiming to be the strongest man in the world, with arms and feet capable of competing with two bulls, and hands capable of lifting a thousand pounds of iron hammers. His wording was unusually exaggerated, claiming that he had not met an opponent in various ports in both northern and southern China. Makarov himself was ignorant, and the Chinese manager who cooperated with him also did not understand the human relations of Beiping society, and stubbornly clung to the psychology of more than ten years ago, wanting to use the words "foreigner" to intimidate all opposition. The widespread social antipathy that arose was, of course, inevitable. On the second day Makarov took the stage at the Central Hotel, Shen Yousan, the leader of Beiping wrestlers (Shen won the championship in wrestling at the National Games last year in the martial arts category), visited him at the Jintai Hotel on Xiheyan Street, demanding a face-to-face wrestling match, otherwise, he should remove the words "the strongest man in the world, invincible in China." Makarov did not understand Chinese. Shen talked to him, but did not get anywhere. The next day, he led a young martial artist, a disciple of his, and visited Makarov again, still demanding a match. Makarov refused again. Shen's disciple saw two iron hammers, said to weigh a thousand pounds, which Makarov had put in the corner of the room, which Makarov used to show off on stage. Shen's disciple then lifted them lightly with an unconcerned attitude, moved them for a long time, and discarded them on the ground. Makarov was greatly frightened when he saw this, expressed humility, and said that a martial arts match might be dangerous and dared not accept the challenge. The next day, Shen brought a bow and arrow that he had hidden at home and visited Makarov alone, saying that if you can draw this bow, you can prove that you really have a thousand-pound broadsword, and there is no need for me to compete with you. If you cannot draw this bow, it proves that all your tricks on stage are magic tricks, and you are here to deceive China for money. This kind of test, you draw the bow for me to see first, and I will draw the bow for you to see later. There is no competition, so there is no danger, and you should happily agree to it, right? When Makarov heard Shen's words, he still resolutely refused, but said that he was willing to cooperate with Shen in performing and making money together. Shen firmly refused. His assistant, the so-called Chinese manager, even said, "If you annoy the foreigner, even if you don't have a martial arts match, he can still beat you up and cause an international dispute, which you cannot bear," and so on. Shen was greatly displeased and angrily told the famous figures in the Beiping martial arts community about the whole affair. So, following Shen, four or five people have sent letters to Makarov to challenge him to a martial arts match and visited him in person to request a test. Makarov felt the pain of coping with them, and the social psychology of Beiping unanimously supported Chinese national quintessence, and believed that Makarov's dare not compete was proof that he was deceiving and had no real strength. As a result, Makarov's business had very few attendees, and as a result, he only sold more than ten yuan a day, and was in a dilemma.

Just as this strongman was trapped in a hotel and preparing to leave the capital, a female general suddenly arrived. She is the daughter of Yang Jiaotou (instructor), a famous martial arts expert and a master of Xingyiquan from Hejian. Her name is Yang Jianxia. Hearing of Makarov's exaggeration, she wanted to express her feelings for Chinese martial arts. She came to Beiping from her hometown specifically to compete. As soon as she got off the car, she wrote to Makarov, saying, "I read in the newspaper yesterday that you boast of being invincible in the world. If you do not have real skills, you would never dare to boast so much. Although I am a woman, I am willing to compete with you to gain experience. If you are willing to teach me, please indicate the location and date. I am looking forward to it very much. Yang Jianxia sends her respects." Makarov did not respond to this letter. The reporter knew that among the Taijiquan experts in northern China, the Chen family from Chenjiagou in Henan was the founder, and the Xingyiquan school regarded Yang Jiaotou from Hejian as the master. His daughter, Jianxia, inherited the family's knowledge from a young age and won the championship by defeating several famous martial artists in the Baoding Martial Arts Competition. All circles in Beiping have long admired her as an extraordinary female knight. Therefore, the reporter rushed to visit her at Dayi Apartment in Piku Hutong. The lady received him. According to the conversation, "I am not particularly good at strength, or I might even be called 'weak' or 'powerless'. However, in the two areas of swordsmanship and internal strength, I was taught the oral formulas by my father, and I can see the metaphysical realm of Chinese martial arts that transcends the physical. The characteristics of Chinese martial arts are very different from Westerners who are as strong as cattle and specialize in wrestling. We not only do not rejoice in great strength, but even regard great strength as a disease. Therefore, limited by this kind of family tradition, I always regard fighting with people as a great taboo. Even if I sometimes try with an enemy, I am psychologically acting with an 'unavoidable' attitude. This time I came to Beiping, I had two missions: (1) Stimulated by the national crisis, I want to contribute my skills to the female compatriots in Beiping by establishing a Xingyiquan Women's Training Institute; (2) Driven by the idea of national self-strengthening, I do not want to let a Russian regard our Chinese people as nothing. This is the great reason why I wrote to Makarov yesterday, violating the taboos of my family tradition." When the lady spoke to this point, the reporter asked again about the scene of the Baoding Martial Arts Competition a few years ago. What technique did she use to fight against several men and throw them all off the "ring"? The lady said, "I first learned swordsmanship and internal strength. My father's most experienced learning is also in this area. Internal strength and sword are the best of metaphysical martial arts. Those who study this path must eventually reach the realm of 'moving with the spirit' to be considered successful. The opposite is true of external styles. No matter how calm and powerful, external styles cannot avoid the pain of tension when fighting with people. Internal styles purely take the attitude of 'waiting for work at ease' and 'controlling movement with stillness'. Therefore, I was able to defeat four or five men by myself at the Baoding Martial Arts Competition. The only reason is that the opponents I encountered at that time were all external styles, even though they were famous martial artists. They had already exhausted their strength when they first fought with me, and I did not have to seek victory, so I did not have to worry about mental exhaustion or consumption. When they weakened again and again, I won in one fell swoop. My consecutive victories against four or five people are better said to be victories with the spirit than with strength. In short, the strength of internal strength lies in this point. This cannot be understood without understanding it spiritually. It is very difficult to understand concretely when describing it verbally." It is said that Ms. Yang is the daughter of Yang, the grand master of "Xingyi" in North China. Her words are so exquisite that they are described in detail for the reference of martial arts experts and enthusiasts of martial arts. (21st)

Songjiang 87

Lost Middle School Students in the Province Found

Cai Zukang and Shen Jiapei, students of Songjiang Middle School in the province, are both 14 years old. Their academic performance is always among the best, and their personalities are also good. Boarding students at the school have a regular holiday every Wednesday. The two students asked for leave to go out at around 5 pm on the 21st, but they did not return that night. The school notified their families and searched together, but they were not found. It was not until today that they were spotted by the road protection soldiers stationed in Shihudang, who questioned them and learned that the students wanted to live in seclusion, support themselves, and did not want to be supported by their families or study. Observing their expressions, it seemed that they had been stimulated. One student lived in Fengjing and was sent back to Fengjing to his family, while the other was escorted back to school by the soldiers.

Local News

Preventing the Export of Silver, Domestic Silver Shipments Require Passports 88

Customs Issues Public Notice on Order of the Ministry of Finance

Large Amounts Shipped Out in Recent Days, Silver Market Extremely Tight

Xin Xin News Agency reports that in order to prevent the large-scale export of silver, the Ministry of Finance increased the export tax on silver on October 15 and established the Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee. The export of silver has gradually decreased. However, with the continued rise in silver prices abroad in recent days, unscrupulous merchants have been shipping silver to the mainland and smuggling it for export, resulting in a sharp increase in silver leaving the country and a tightening of the silver market. The Ministry of Finance specifically ordered the Jianghai Customs on the 22nd that all domestic shipments of silver must have a passport from the Ministry of Finance before they can be shipped. The details are recorded as follows:

Customs Issues Public Notice Requiring Passports for Silver Shipments

Tang Hai'an, Superintendent of Jianghai Customs, and Robert Bredon, Commissioner of Customs, jointly issued a notice stating: In order to issue a public notice, in accordance with the order of the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance, starting from November 21 of this year, all banks must have their passports from the Ministry of Finance inspected by the customs when transporting whole boxes or bags of silver coins domestically before they can be shipped. Those who transport without passports will be regarded as smuggling, and the goods will be confiscated in accordance with regulations. All merchants are hereby notified.

Preventing Unscrupulous Merchants from Smuggling for Export

A reporter from Xin Xin News Agency learned from banking circles yesterday that recently, mainland agricultural products, such as cotton and grains, have been harvested and traded on the market, requiring the use of silver. Therefore, in recent days, silver coins have been shipped from Shanghai to various mainland ports, such as Hankou, Tianjin, Beiping, Shantou, Xiamen, Qinhuangdao, Qingdao, and Yantai, in large quantities. From the 1st to the 15th of this month, it is estimated that about 3.54 million yuan was shipped. However, some merchants, motivated by profit, saw that silver prices abroad were still higher than those in the country, so they took this opportunity to transfer silver to the mainland and then smuggle it for export in order to make profits. In order to prevent smuggling for export, the Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee, in addition to requesting the Ministry of Finance to order all customs offices that domestic shipments of silver must have passports from the Ministry of Finance before they can be shipped, also carefully considered the balancing tax announced at 10 am every day before deciding to announce it, with the intention of reducing smuggling. At the same time, Guangdong, Sichuan, Gansu, and other provinces have also issued orders prohibiting the export of silver to prevent unscrupulous merchants from smuggling.

Silver Discount Rises Sharply by 25 Cents

Recently, the silver discount in the city has risen sharply from 15 cents to 25 cents due to the sharp increase in silver coin exports, the reduction in silver reserves, and the increasingly tight silver market. This is a phenomenon that has not been seen in years. Usually, during the autumn and winter seasons when agricultural products are launched on the market, the silver discount is higher than in the spring and summer seasons due to the need for silver in various places, but it has never been as high as 25 cents this year. This is also affected by the large-scale export of silver. According to financial circles, after the Customs announces that domestic shipments of silver coins must have passports from the Ministry of Finance before they can be shipped, the silver discount is expected to fall back.

Another Huge Amount of Silver Shipped to the United States Today 89

Paying More Than 70,000 Yuan in Export Tax

Yesterday, a certain foreign bank reported the shipment of one million yuan in silver, all of which were Chinese national coins, divided into 200 boxes. In the afternoon, it contacted the Dalae Foreign Company to entrust the Lincoln Presidential ship to leave Shanghai today and ship the silver to New York, USA. It paid 77,500 yuan in export tax in accordance with the new regulations. This is the fourth batch of silver shipped out after China increased its silver tariffs.

Sichuan Fellow Provincials Telegraph the Central Government and Liu Xiang to Stop Communist Bandits from Fleeing to Sichuan 91

Expeditiously Rectify Sichuan Politics

The Shanghai Sichuan Fellow Provincials Association held an emergency executive committee meeting at its office yesterday. More than ten people attended, including Li Xunfu, Zhang Shulin, Qiu Zhizhong, Deng Youguang, Zhong Hangsu, Wen Disheng, Tang Zhonghou, Liu Xueqiao, Wu Youdan, and Tan Jiqing. The meeting was chaired by Zhong Hangsu, and many important matters were resolved. Two telegrams were drafted on the spot and presented to the Central Government and Liu Xiang, requesting their adoption and implementation. The original telegrams are recorded as follows:

To the Central Government Telegram, Urgent. Respected Chairman Lin of Nanjing, Chairman Chiang, and President Wang, Communist bandits have been fleeing to Sichuan for two years. Due to military, political, and financial relations, not only has Kuang's banditry in northern Sichuan not been wiped out, but various communist bandits such as Xiao, He, Zhu, and Mao are also likely to take the opportunity to enter Sichuan and join forces. Our association believes that this serious problem is not a local issue in Sichuan, but a key to the survival of the entire Chinese nation. Therefore, we convened an emergency executive committee meeting today and immediately resolved to contribute five measures to the Central Government for suppressing the bandits and securing Sichuan: (1) Please send a senior military officer from the Central Government to sit in western China, provide instructions to various provinces on bandit suppression strategies at any time, and clearly define rewards and punishments to implement supervision; (2) Please urgently telegraph the Shaanxi army to immediately dispatch a large army to northern Sichuan to cooperate with the various Sichuan bandit suppression armies, with the aim of achieving a pincer attack; (3) Please instruct the leaders of Hunan, Hubei, Guangxi, and Guizhou to encircle the main force of the communist bandits fleeing westward and send a large army to intercept them to prevent them from fleeing into Sichuan and joining forces with Kuang, Xiao, He, and other bandits; (4) Please earnestly begin to rectify Sichuan's finances and统筹统支 (统筹统支 is difficult to translate exactly, but it roughly means 'centrally plan and allocate') bandit suppression military expenses; (5) Please expedite the promotion of Sichuan politics in accordance with the principle of 30% military affairs and 70% political affairs. The above five points are simple methods for suppressing bandits and securing Sichuan. Our association believes that the current situation is urgent, like eggs piled on top of each other. We feel the danger and dare not remain silent. We hope that you will adopt our suggestions, and Sichuan's future and the nation's future will both benefit. We are sending this telegram with trepidation and look forward to your clear instructions. Sichuan Fellow Provincials Association respectfully.

To Liu Xiang Telegram, Urgent. Respected Supervisor Liu of Nanjing, you were able to come to Beijing resolutely to petition the Central Government, which is what our association sympathizes with. However, our association believes that this opportunity is serious and critical, and we cannot remain silent, nor do we dare to remain silent. We have convened an emergency meeting today to offer several opinions: (1) Please immediately reorganize and equip the various bandit suppression armies in Sichuan and strictly order all the previous commanders who avoided their duties to atone for their crimes, otherwise, they will be removed from their posts and punished first; (2) Please issue a mobilization order immediately and establish contact with the Shaanxi army. If the various Sichuan commanders are still hesitant and do not move forward, then they will be punished by military law; (3) Please telegraph the leaders of Hunan, Hubei, Guangxi, and Guizhou provinces to strike head-on at the communist bandits, wipe them out together, and prevent Zhu Mao's main force from occupying Sichuan and causing trouble to the whole country; (4) Please thoroughly investigate the financial staff and replace those who are not capable. If anyone has embezzled previous bandit suppression military pay, they will be dismissed and ordered to compensate. Future military pay must be used on the soldiers. If there are any cases of embezzlement or deductions, they will be punished by military law; (5) Please order the commanders of all armies under your command to immediately abolish all kinds of exorbitant taxes and strictly prohibit the pre-collection of taxes; (6) Please encourage the export of Sichuan's local products and promote them abroad, and exempt them from taxes to facilitate promotion, offset imports, and save the economic crisis; (7) Please restore student loans and, for students who remit tuition fees out of Sichuan, please instruct all banks to waive remittance fees if the fees are certified by the schools and local educational institutions. All the above points are important matters. Since you were able to come to Beijing with awareness, you should be able to accept the public opinion of our association with sincerity. We hope that you will give us detailed instructions. Sichuan Fellow Provincials Association respectfully.

Shanghai County Starts Winter Defense Early 94

County Government Convenes a Meeting

Resolves Various Measures

Shanghai County originally planned to start winter defense on December 1. However, due to the frequent occurrence of theft cases in the county, in order to maintain local tranquility, it was decided to start early and issue a notice yesterday to implement it immediately. The county government convened a winter defense meeting, attended by Xu Yuyin, Director of the Public Security Bureau, Lu Zhongyu, Commander of the First Security Squadron, and Wu Shifang, Li You, Tian Wang Chengyao, Fu Dianying, and Xing Zhigang, Directors of various districts. Wang Xuepeng, Director of the First Section of the County Government, was present. The meeting was chaired by Pan Zhongjia, the County Magistrate, and the minutes were recorded by Cao Yuanxun. The following measures were discussed and resolved: (1) Each district shall convene and organize its own winter defense office; (2) The winter defense period is scheduled for four months; (3) During the winter defense period, inspections shall be carried out on major land and water transportation routes and public places; (4) The local watchmen and the police team shall coordinate their defense efforts, which shall be decided by the winter defense offices in each district; (5) Crack down on vagrants in various places. If there are any suspicious or unemployed vagrants, they shall be sent to the vagrant skills training center for accommodation; (6) Request the assistance of the First District of the Water Public Security in protecting the waterways along the banks; (7) Pass the plans for joint defense, sentry duty, and patrolling proposed by the security team; (8) Pass the police force deployment plan carried out by the public security security team; (9) Xinda Kiln in the Second District will stop work during the winter. All workers who stay and do not disperse are likely to cause trouble. The Public Security Bureau should formulate joint guarantee measures to order the workers of the factory to obtain special joint guarantee forms and conduct inspections at any time. If there are any undesirable elements, they will be deported; (10) The township chiefs in each district shall be instructed to advise the villagers that, in the event of a theft, they should immediately sound the alarm and report to the local public security authorities to send police to patrol and arrest. In the future, if military and police officers go to the countryside for on-site inspections, any requests for supplies shall be reported by the public at any time for strict punishment.

Four Provinces' Match Industry Implements Merger 95

Preparations are underway, and a preparatory office has been established and is actively proceeding

Named the Greater China Match Co., Ltd.

Xinxin News Agency reports: Our country's domestic match industry has recently been experiencing overproduction and a sharp drop in market prices, causing considerable panic among the industry. Consequently, Sun Runzhai of the China Match Factory and others, in addition to requesting government relief, also sought self-improvement measures within the industry, leading to the proposal of merging the operations of eight factories in four provinces. Recognizing the significant impact of this matter on the future of domestic goods, the Xinxin News Agency reporter paid a special visit to Gao Songfu, a magnate in the match industry. According to Mr. Gao, the situation is as follows:

Consulting on Relief: Mr. Gao first stated that, in recent years, the industry has seen the rise of new factories, resulting in annual production exceeding demand. Products from various factories have been stockpiling, and the abundance of inventory in the market has led to a continuous decline in wholesale prices, causing considerable anxiety within the industry. Subsequently, initiated by Sun Runzhai of the China Match Factory, various industry peers were invited to convene a series of joint meetings to discuss relief measures. It was decided to request government assistance and to formulate four measures for the authorities to adopt and implement, including: (1) Requesting restrictions on the establishment of new factories, as the existing match factories nationwide are sufficient for current needs. Adding new factories would inevitably lead to oversupply, so the government should restrict them. (2) Requesting restrictions on production to ensure supply and demand are balanced. (3) Requesting limitations on sales regions. (4) Requesting price controls. Regarding the above four points, the government has agreed to implement the feasible ones as soon as possible.

Unified Operations: Regarding the industry's collective efforts for self-rescue, apart from the method of merging operations, there is no other better solution. Joint sales by industry members can avoid industry competition and hidden price drops, which is unified operations. This allows for planned organization and external sales. Consequently, the industry in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Hubei provinces has joined forces, including eight factories: Nantong Tong Sui, Ningbo Zhengda, Linhuai Huai Shang, Hankou Chu Sheng, Shanghai Hua Ming, China, Da Ming, and Da Hua. They have merged to form the preparatory office of the Greater China Match Co., Ltd., and Mr. He Shichang of Zhengda Factory has been appointed as the head of the preparatory office to actively promote the process.

Merger Outline: The company's merger outline has been passed and is recorded as follows: Article 1: This merger involves dissolving the old companies and forming a new company, named the Greater China Match Co., Ltd., with a tentatively set capital of one million national currency. The merged companies will retain their original names. When the company is registered, the original names of the merged companies will be attached for registration. Article 2: After the merger of each company, all original stocks will be invalidated. The number of shares to be received in the new company shall be based on the net value of the total original assets of each company (hereinafter referred to as net assets, i.e., the result of subtracting liabilities from fixed and current assets). Article 3: Regarding the method of asset valuation, all assets of each factory will be divided into fixed assets and current assets. Fixed assets, such as depreciation of factory buildings, machinery, and equipment, and the price of land, and current assets, such as raw materials and finished products, will be fairly valued by the valuation committee. If there is disagreement, a neutral person will be asked to arbitrate. Article 4: Accounts receivable from each company, excluding bad debts, may be included in the calculation of current assets. Article 5: All liabilities of each company shall be settled independently. The company may retroactively recognize any existing items and original credit loans. Article 6: The valuation committee shall be determined by the preparatory committee, with one person from each factory and two additional neutral persons. Separate detailed rules will be set for the valuation of each factory's assets. Article 7: Regarding the identification of trademarks, each company has numerous original trademarks. After the merger, the reputable ones will be retained, and unnecessary ones will be deleted as appropriate. After the existing trademarks are used up, the words "Supervised by Greater China Match Co., Ltd." should be added to the original trademark to indicate identification. Article 8: This merger will continue to lease the rented factories, houses, and land from the company. Article 9: If the company needs them, the company may inherit and merge any subsidiary assets of each factory. Article 10: The company will employ the original employees of each company according to their abilities. Article 11: If there are any matters not covered in this outline, they should be discussed jointly by each factory and added or deleted at any time.

Minsheng Company's Self-Built Minquan New Steamer Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 96

The largest steamer in the Sichuan River cost a total of 200,000 yuan

Will set sail on the Shanghai-Chongqing line as soon as the deck is installed

The new steamer Minquan, built by Minsheng Industrial Company, arrived in Shanghai from Chongqing yesterday morning and berthed at the Longmao Wharf in Pudong. It was decided to install the deck in Shanghai and then sail on the Shanghai-Chongqing line when the water rises. The details are as follows:

Self-Built Process: On March 5th of last year, Minsheng Company purchased the hull of the Wanliu steamer from the British Taikoo Shipping Company for 500 Shanghai taels. The Wanliu steamer had run aground and sunk at the Chaipanzi area above Changshou on the Sichuan River. After two days of rescue efforts, it was finally salvaged. On May 19th of the same year, it was towed back by the Minkang steamer and berthed at the Minsheng Company Shipyard in Qingcaobao, Sichuan. Construction began in January of this year to lengthen the hull. It took more than ten months to complete and was named the Minquan.

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday: The Minquan steamer is 219 feet 11 inches long, 31 feet wide, 10 feet deep, has a draft of 8 feet 4 inches, a speed of approximately 13.5 miles per hour, a gross tonnage of approximately 1,200 tons, and a net tonnage of approximately 700 tons. It is the largest steamer on the Sichuan River, costing approximately 200,000 yuan to build. After completion, it sailed from Chongqing to Shanghai on the 4th of this month, carrying cargo. It stopped at various ports, such as Wanxian and Hankou, to load and unload passengers and goods. It arrived in Shanghai at 9 a.m. yesterday.

Welcoming the New Steamer: After arriving in Shanghai, it berthed at the Longmao Wharf in Pudong. The shipowner is Zhou Haiqing, and the manager (i.e., compradore) is Weng Jingxun. Upon arrival in Shanghai, Zhang Shulin, the manager of the Shanghai branch of Minsheng Company, led all the staff to Pudong Wharf to welcome the steamer. A large number of firecrackers were prepared and set off upon arrival. The deck of the steamer has not yet been installed and will be installed in Shanghai at an estimated cost of 30,000 to 40,000 yuan.

History of the Minquan: When the Minquan steamer first entered the Sichuan River in the early years of the Republic of China, it was named Longmao and was owned by the British Longmao Foreign Company. At that time, it was 204 feet long, 31 feet wide, 10 feet deep, had a draft of 8 feet 2 inches, a speed of 14.5 miles per hour, a gross tonnage of 1,112 tons, and a registered tonnage of 671 tons. It was built by the Shanghai Jiangnan Shipyard in 1920. It began sailing to Sichuan in June of the Republic of China. Due to careless navigation, it crashed into a rock in the Yichang Gorge. On November 24th of the same year, it sailed to Shanghai for repairs. In 1924, Longmao sold it to Taikoo, and it was renamed Wanliu. In 1926, it caused the Wanxian Massacre. On May 31st, 1931, it ran aground in the Chaipanzi area above Changshou. It was submerged due to rising water. After several days, the Taikoo Foreign Company and insurance company deemed it impossible to salvage, so the Taikoo Foreign Company sold it to Minsheng Company.

Sanbei New Steamer Xinpu Scheduled to Sail the Yangtze River 97

In order to strengthen its transportation capacity, Sanbei Company purchased four merchant steamers. The Xinpu steamer, which has been received from Hong Kong and repaired, has a load capacity of 1,850 tons and can sail both in rivers and seas. After Sanbei purchased it, it added cabins, and the hull was completely renovated. It has now left the factory and is scheduled to replace the Xinxing service on the Yangtze River on the 27th of this month.
