Record of the Opening of the Wuhua Bank Lawsuit 104

The defendant stated that the debt could be repaid

The court must summon three representatives from the head office to inquire

After the Shanghai branch of Wuhua Industrial Bank, located at 130 Ningbo Road in the Public Concession, and the Baxianqiao branch in the French Concession closed simultaneously on August 21 of this year, the Shanghai branch immediately appointed lawyers Wu Kaisheng, Jiang Yiping, Chen Chengyin, and accountants Jiang Wanping, Wang Sifang, and Chen Xianmo to announce the liquidation. The Guangzhou Wuhua Bank head office also sent three representatives, Xu Yuangao, Huang Linsheng, and Yang Yigong, to Shanghai to act as full agents, appointing lawyers Luo Jiaheng and Pan Zhenya, and accountant Li Zheng to liquidate. The two sides argued and published in newspapers, starting a pen war. Subsequently, ten households, including depositors and debtors of the two banks, Zhu Longgen and Chen Xianji, separately extended lawyers Zhang Shijie, Lou Yunmei, Mao Fengwu, and Xu Jie to file a criminal complaint with the Second Special District Court, accusing the branch's deputy managers Fan Shaoliang and Ye Haitian, the branch's deputy managers Wang Jian'e and Wu Yousan, the branch's assistant managers Xie Shunzhi and Tang Songshan, and the consultants Tang Shoumin and Chen Bingqian of fraud, requesting that they be interrogated according to law. According to the complaint, the court once summoned them on September 26, but the defendants did not arrive and the date was changed. The details have been recorded in previous reports. At 3:30 p.m. yesterday, judge Xiong Huiping, accompanied by clerk Tao Zongkan, specially opened the second criminal court to hear the case. The ten plaintiffs, Zhu Longgen, etc. (the names have been detailed in previous reports), each arrived with their lawyers. Except for Chen Bingqian, who was recuperating in Moganshan and appointed a lawyer as an agent, all the defendants arrived with their defense lawyers Wu Kaisheng, Hua Maosheng, and Zheng Wenkai. First, the plaintiff Zhu Longgen stated that he accused the defendants of opening a bank without registering with the government, using several years of planning as a fraudulent means to deceive people into depositing savings, and breaching trust by using advertisements to deceive depositors. I deposited money at the Baxianqiao branch. The official asked Fan and Ye if they were the deputy managers of the branch, and Xie and Tang were the assistant managers and consultants. What does your deposit at the branch have to do with the other six people? He replied, their branches are connected and closed. The night before the closure, they hired a car to move the branch's belongings. There are rumors to that effect. At this point, the plaintiff's agent, lawyer Lou Yunmei, stated that it was found that the moving of the belongings was done by Xiangsheng Motor Company, numbers 18498 and 18491. At that time, there was also an accountant from the branch who was detained by the police. The defendant's lawyer, Wu Kaisheng, stated that the police had investigated this matter at that time, and because there was no criminal relationship, it was not accepted. He requested the court to investigate with the police. The official then asked the remaining plaintiffs, who all stated that their opinions were the same as what Zhu Longgen said. Some of the money was deposited in the branch, and some in the branch. Now they demand the return of the money and request that it be handled according to law, etc. At this point, the official questioned the manager of the defendant branch, Wang Jian'e, who stated that he had no right to inquire about registration. The branch sent me to be the manager of the branch. The reason for the closure was that the branch's financial turnover was not working well. The branch also closed because it could not be maintained. The branch has a capital of 500,000, and the head office in Guangzhou has a capital of about 2 million. Other branches are still operating normally. After the closure of the Shanghai branch, the head office sent three representatives, Xu Yuangao, Huang Linsheng, and Yang Yigong, to Shanghai to fully liquidate and repay the debts. The accounts of the public and branch have been cleared. After offsetting the income and expenditure, there is still a surplus of more than 100,000. The first step now is to repay the savings, and the second step is to repay the current deposits, which can be fully repaid in the future. Now, the two houses must be topped out, etc. Then, the branch manager Fan Shaoliang testified that he was the manager of the branch and the head office was registered in Hong Kong. The official said, you should also register in Shanghai. He replied, this is the right of the head office. Asked, what is the reason for this closure? He replied, because the income and payment turnover cannot be offset, resulting in the closure. However, there is more than 100,000 owed on the accounts, but there is no actual loss. Now the liquidation office has notified the debtors to recover the debts. The branch's houses have been topped out, and more than 20,000 gold have been obtained. In my opinion, savings can be repaid in the shortest time, more than a month, and current deposits can also be repaid by the end of the lunar year. Moreover, the branch's debts are the responsibility of the head office and must be repaid. Regarding whether to resume business in the future, the right is with the head office, I cannot say. Then asked the two deputy managers of the branch, Ye Haitian and Wu Yousan, who replied that their meaning was the same as what Wang and Fan said. Xie Shunzhi testified that although he was the assistant manager of the branch, his position was equal to that of a staff member. He now hopes that the head office will be responsible for the liquidation. Tang Songshan testified that he was the assistant manager of the branch and was not responsible for the branch's affairs. Because above the assistant manager, there are also treasurers and consultants. Tang Shoumin testified that Fan Shaoliang asked me to serve as a consultant. In fact, he had never been to the bank, and Fan had never asked me, so I don't know the details. However, the consultant's position is only advisory. At this point, the court stated that it still needs to investigate the case and must summon the three representatives sent by the head office for liquidation. It then announced that it would be scheduled to summon and hear the case again, and then adjourned.

Central Bank to Undertake Construction of Qoukiang Wharf 106

Construction Cost of Three Million, Expanding Original Plan

Special Committee Formed for Design, Construction to Begin Soon

Upon Completion, Jianghai Customs Plans to Relocate for Office

Qoukiang Wharf, the only great building in the city center area, after the municipal government completed its planning, was originally intended to begin construction immediately. However, due to limited funding, it has been delayed until now and has not yet been realized. Recently, the Central Bank believed that after the completion of the wharf, ships entering the Huangpu River from overseas in the future could be completely docked there, which would not only benefit water conservancy and commerce, but also prosper the market. It would have a great relationship with business, transportation, economy, and so on, so it was very happy to invest. Now, it has been decided that the Central Bank will undertake the project and form a special committee to proceed. Its plan is even greater than that approved by the municipal government, costing about more than three million, and it can be regarded as the only major project in the customs aspect of our country. The details obtained are as follows:

Bank Investment Qoukiang Wharf is one of the major constructions in the city center area. In recent years, the municipal government has been working hard on the construction work in the city center area. For example, the municipal hospital, swimming pool, sports field, sports field, municipal park, etc., have all started construction one after another. However, although there is determination for the construction of Qoukiang Wharf, the project is very great, and the stipulated funding reaches two million yuan. After the January 28th Incident in Shanghai, the municipal government's income suddenly decreased significantly, and there was no surplus funds to seek construction. Therefore, the construction of this Qoukiang Wharf was virtually suspended. Recently, the Central Bank believed that after the completion of the wharf, ship transportation would be concentrated in the area and the market would prosper, which is also expected. Therefore, it is willing to invest in undertaking the project. It has been in contact with the municipal government several times and has reached an agreement.

Construction to Begin Soon The Central Bank believes that Qoukiang Wharf will be the only intermediary agency for developing the commercial economy of the city center area in the future, so it has great hope. According to the original plan of the municipal government, the cost of constructing Qoukiang Wharf is a total of two million. The bank intends to expand the original plan of the municipal government, increase construction costs, and improve various equipment. Now the estimated construction cost is about three to four million yuan, and a special committee has been organized to carry out this matter, and construction will begin soon.

Bird's-eye View of the Situation Qoukiang Wharf is in the middle of the Huangpu River, northeast of Yangshupu Jungong Road. The land is the deepest part of the entire Huangpu River. The river surface is wide, and any large wheel can be docked. On one side, it can be connected to Songhu Road and Sanmin Road, and on the other side, it controls the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River. The terrain is quite majestic.

Customs Relocation The Jianghai Customs is currently considering a major issue, that is, after the completion of Qoukiang Wharf, it may relocate there, which is not yet known. The current overseas rounds entering can only stop at Yangshupu Wharf. If they enter further, because the small wheels south of Yangshupu are as dense as stars, there is a risk of collision from time to time. The river surface is narrow and cannot turn around, so it cannot directly enter the abdomen. Therefore, if a large wheel arrives in Shanghai, the customs must send a small wheel from the new customs wharf to pick up and drop off, which is very inconvenient. If Qoukiang Wharf is built, all ships will directly dock at the wharf, because that place is the first wharf to enter from the Wusongkou. The entry of giant ships can reduce the itinerary, and passengers can directly disembark without the need for small wheels to pick up and drop off, which is very convenient. At the same time, all loading, unloading, and goods will also be at the wharf. If Jianghai Customs is still at the new customs, its tax revenue will be greatly reduced. Therefore, after the establishment of Qoukiang Wharf, Jianghai Customs may also relocate to the area for office.

Assassination Case on Dongxin Bridge Street, Two Brothers Suffer Tragic Deaths Together 108

A Sharp Kitchen Knife Inserted into the Younger Brother's Neck, He is Already Dead

The Elder Brother with Seven Knife Wounds All Over His Body is Also in Critical Condition

—The Inside Story Has Not Yet Been Ascertained—

At 4:45 yesterday morning, when the sky had not yet dawned, a bizarre murder occurred in Building 34 of Chongde Fang, a newly built building at the intersection of Dongxin Bridge Street and Minguo Road in the French Concession. The victims were two brothers from other places living in Shanghai. The younger brother's head had been chopped off, and the elder brother was seriously injured and his life was also in critical condition. The details are recorded below:

Brothers Living Together There are more than a dozen newly built three-story houses at the intersection of Fahua Minguo Road at the southern end of Dongxin Bridge Street, French Concession. The lane is named Chongde Fang, and the house number 24 in the lane is a single three-story house, which is leased by Dai Chen, a local woman who sets up a fish stall in the Caishi Street. In addition to living in the living room downstairs, the remaining rooms upstairs are rented to others. A year ago, two brothers from Henan, Zhang Guanghua (26 years old) and Zhang Guangzhou (18 years old), rented the pavilion room on the second floor of the house.

Calling for Help According to Zhang Guanghua, he worked in the Navigation Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation, and his brother Guangzhou was studying at a school in Shanghai. The two brothers went out early and returned late, without any other differences. The friends who came and went were also very few. But until about 5:00 yesterday morning, French police officer No. 455, Yue Pu, was patrolling the lane with a gun and suddenly heard a loud cry for help from house No. 24. He immediately informed Yue Pu No. 194 and Chinese police officers No. 644 and No. 380, and ran to the nearby iron fence patrol booth to report to the police station.

One Dead and One Injured The police chief immediately sent a large number of Chinese and foreign detectives to arrive. When they entered the house, they saw Zhang Guanghua lying down on the awning of the stove room, covered in blood and dying. When they went to the pavilion room on the second floor to check, they saw the room door was tightly closed, so they rushed in together. They saw Guangzhou lying naked and stiff on the ground, with blood all over the ground. A sharp kitchen knife was still inserted into his neck. The skull had been broken, and only an inch or so of flesh was connected. He had already died. The detectives checked the house and found more than one hundred yuan in banknotes and foreign currency in the wallet, and a few tables and chairs, but nothing else.

The Injured with Seven Knives After the detectives finished the examination, they inquired from the neighbors living in the same house. They all said that they were all sleeping. When they heard the cry for help and came out to see, the tragedy had already been done, and the murderer was nowhere to be seen. The detectives quickly used a car to send Guanghua to Renji Hospital for treatment. It was found that he had a total of seven knives on his body, including five knives on his head, one knife on the neck and one on the right ear. Guangzhou's body was taken away by the coroner's office to wait for the Second Special Court to examine it. At 11:00 noon, Prosecutor Wang Ren came to the office and confirmed that he died of knife wounds. He then summoned witnesses Yan Jintao and Dai Rongxiang, the son of the second landlord, for questioning.

Four or Five Murderers Then the detective presented a murder weapon to the case. The official stated that the deceased had no family members in Shanghai and instructed the hall to handle the burial. The police station sent detectives to Renji Hospital to inquire about Zhang Guanghua's situation at that time. It was said that at that time, four or five thugs broke into the pavilion room, and without saying a word, they raised their axes and chopped at the two of us. I escaped by jumping out of the window, but I was seriously injured. As for how my brother died, I don't know. However, the police station believed that the case was bizarre and conducted a thorough investigation in all directions. It was faintly heard that Zhang Guanghua had been fired from the Navigation Administration Bureau the day before.

Sheng Yu Chang is Sued Again for Abandonment 109

The Yan Shuang Qin Case Has Ended

The Lin Yu Jin Matter Arises Again

Sheng Yuchang, the grandson of Sheng Xuanhuai, a former Qing Dynasty official, who currently resides at No. 1 Beidang Road, French Concession, fell in love with Yan Shuangqin, the daughter of Yan Minghan, a Taoist priest living in Kang Nai Tuo Road, and lived together for nearly three years. Until the year before last, the love between the two suddenly broke down, and the two separated immediately. Yan Shuangqin and her parents, with the qualifications of legal representatives, jointly hired a lawyer to sue Sheng Yuchang for abandonment in the Second Special District Court. After several court hearings, until July of last year, the relationship was restored, and a unconditional reconciliation was reached. The Yan party withdrew the lawsuit and the case was closed. Now, Lin Yujin has hired a lawyer to file a complaint with the criminal court of the Second Special Court, suing Sheng Yuchang for abandonment. Upon receiving the complaint, the court has issued a summons and notified both parties to appear in the Second Criminal Court at 2:00 pm today to hear the case. It is estimated that Criminal Court Chief Wang Gangxu will still hear the case.

Scheme to Pick up Iron Sheets Results in Over 4,000 Gold Being Swindled Away 110

Rong Changnian Escapes Without a Trace

Zhu Fuxiang Cannot Shirk Responsibility

Qin Ziwei, the comprador of the packing factory of the French-Shang Yongxing Foreign Firm in Lujiazui, Pudong, purchased iron sheets for packing from Jifeng Iron Firm at No. 671 Zhejiang Road in May of this year through the solicitation of Rong Changnian, a hardware broker, for a total of 6,700 yuan. The usual procedure for picking up goods is that Qin pays the money and then exchanges the payment at Jifeng Iron Firm for the bill of lading to pick up the goods. On the 2nd of this month, there were still iron sheets worth 4,109 yuan that had not been picked up. Qin then sent his partner Jiang Ruifu to take the passbook to the Nanjing Road Bund wharf on the afternoon of the 2nd of this month, while he was disembarking. Unexpectedly, the broker Rong Changnian was already waiting at the wharf. After talking with Jiang, he asked Jiang whether he had brought the money. Jiang replied that he had brought it. The two talked as they walked. Rong claimed to Jiang that the bill of lading for the iron sheets had been mortgaged to the Shanghai Bank. Now that he wanted to pick up the goods, he had to redeem the bill of lading from the Shanghai Bank. He instructed Jiang to wait at the Shanghai Bank market, and he would come later. After saying that, they parted ways. Jiang then exchanged 4,109 yuan of Zhuang tickets at Baodayu Money Shop, which he had been dealing with, and went to the Shanghai Bank to wait. Before long, Rong also arrived. There was also a man in a suit who arrived later. Rong introduced him and pointed out that the man in the suit was Mr. Pan, the owner of Jifeng Iron Firm, and now he could hand over the money so that he could exchange the bill of lading to pick up the goods. Jiang believed it to be true at the time and handed the Zhuang tickets to Rong Changnian, who handed them over to Pan. Pan took the tickets and entered the glass door of the Shanghai Bank's inner room. Jiang and Rong waited outside. Because they had been waiting for a long time and did not see Pan come out, Jiang asked Rong, and Rong's words were ambiguous. Finally, he said that Pan had returned to the store, and he would inquire by phone. He went to the telephone room of the bank together. Unexpectedly, in a blink of an eye, Rong also disappeared. It was then that Jiang realized that he had been deceived, and he quickly telegraphed his comprador Qin Ziwei for instructions. Qin heard the report and telegraphed Baodayu Money Shop to stop payment. The shop claimed that the Zhuang tickets had been checked and cleared by Tongqing Money Shop, and 3,000 yuan had been transferred. Qin then went to Jifeng Iron Firm with Mr. Jiang Ruifu to investigate and learned that all the statements made by Rong were false. He immediately went to Tongqing Shop to inquire. It was said that the Zhuang tickets were entrusted to them by Shengtai Shop, which had been dealing with them, to collect on their behalf. Later, it was found that Shengtai Shop was located at No. 1308 Liuhefang, Roberts Road, and was opened by Zhu Fuxiang (also known as Zhu Lirang), the general affairs section of the Fuxin Tobacco Company, who was from Wuxi. He also went to Zhu's place to investigate and reported to the General Patrol Room, ordering Chinese detective Song Bingzheng and Western detective Beibeining to investigate. He then petitioned the First Special Court to issue a summons. Yesterday morning, Zhu Fuxiang, the owner of Shengtai Shop, was summoned to the Second Criminal Court. Qian Xunjiu, the police lawyer, stated the above situation, and said that according to Jiang Ruifu's statement to the police station, the defendant Zhu Fuxiang was the person who impersonated Mr. Pan, the owner of Jifeng Iron Firm. Now Rong Changnian has escaped without a trace, and the police station has petitioned your court to issue an arrest warrant. The defendant was prosecuted according to Article 363 of the Criminal Law. According to Jiang Ruifu's confession, he was deceived, and he pointed out in court that Zhu Fuxiang was the person who impersonated Mr. Pan at that time, so he was indeed a joint fraud. According to Qin Qianwei's younger brother Qin Qianxiang's complaint about everything, the defendant Zhu Fuxiang denied impersonating the owner of Jifeng Firm, and said that he had been dealing with Rong Changnian for several years. Shengtai Shop was set up by him personally for the purpose of dealing with shame. Because Rong had discounted Zhuang tickets with him several times in the past, he gave Rong 800 yuan in cash and another 3,000 yuan withdrawn from Tongqing Money Shop, and another 300 yuan was deducted from Rong's old debt. He did not know about the fraud. He hired lawyer Jiang Baoli to defend him. Judge Huang verified the confession and ordered Zhu to pay a guarantee of 10,000 yuan and reschedule the trial in seven days.

Founder Zhang Yongnian Reported to the Press Yesterday

Pay a Deposit of Several Hundred Yuan to Order a House

Zhang Yongnian, the founder of Rose Garden New Village of China New Village Construction Society, hosted a banquet for the local press and picture periodical editors at Yizhixiang Western Restaurant last night. More than a hundred people, including reporters from various newspapers and editors from various picture periodicals, attended the banquet, and the host and guests enjoyed themselves. In recent years, Shanghai has experienced soaring land prices and expensive rents, which have been increasing day by day. Residents spend more than one-third of their income on rent, and it is still difficult to obtain a comfortable and clean house. As for purchasing land to build their own houses, it is even beyond the ability of ordinary people. Therefore, housing has become a very serious problem. Mr. Zhang is planning to solve the housing problem for the public. He specially founded Rose Garden New Village in Shanghai.

The first person to create new village construction publicly, since the plan was made public, has been deeply appreciated by people from all walks of life. The first step of its plan, to build houses, has reached its quota, and bidding for construction has already begun. It is expected to be completed in August of next year. However, the implementation of the first step of the plan is to open up a new environment for the middle class, and those who love new village life still regret that it cannot fully meet the economic capabilities of most people. Therefore, they all request the society to

Popularize the benefits of the new village letters and those who personally go to the society to negotiate, there must be dozens of cases every day. The society has always had three standards for new village construction as its goal: (1) For the perfection and detail of the equipment, all public equipment such as transportation, water and electricity, security, market, park, grand auditorium, etc., and public undertakings such as education, health, cooperation, entertainment, etc., are repeatedly concerned; (2) For the economic and comfortable design, the base is square and neat, the residence is perfect, the road is flat and wide, the planting must be pleasing to the eye, and the management is meticulous. One is

Easy to order and build Residents can consider their own economic capabilities, agree on a deadline, and pay monthly, similar to after the rent expires, they can also obtain the ownership of the ordered building and real estate. The society has now decided to follow the needs and requirements of the majority of people in society and contribute the second step of the popularization plan that has been planned for a long time to the society in advance. It is scheduled to be officially announced on the 27th of this month. The various designs of this popularization plan are all for the residents.

Think from their perspective In addition to ordering, there are also fixed-building leasing methods. With a down payment and a deposit of several hundred yuan, you can order a house. The base and house are twice as large as the Shanghai lane-style house, and the monthly rent is only fifty or sixty yuan. If you pay the rent for up to ten or twelve years, you can obtain the ownership of the real estate. From now on, people from all walks of life can solve their housing problems forever in the most economical and simple way. How happy is this! After hearing this report, the people in the press felt that the society was indeed based on the spirit of service, and the intention of reforming the unlimited rental system for people was excellent. Xu Zhuodai, Qian Cangshuo, Mi Xingru, and Yan Duhe, etc., stood up and gave speeches to encourage and encourage them. It was not until about 9:00 pm that they all dispersed happily. The society's new address is No. 1918 Aiduya Road (opposite Nanjing Grand Theater), telephone number 94965.

Barely a Husband and Wife in Name, Never any Bedroom Pleasure 112

Yao Yanping and Xu Jingqing Have Deep Antipathy

Repeated Lawsuits and Reconciliations, Now Sued Again

Yao Yanping, the young owner of Yitai Money Shop in Tilanshui, married Xu Jingqing as his wife, which has been six years. Because Yao's body is hunched over, and there is some kind of relationship in physiology, it is difficult for Xu to be with her spouse for a long time. She only has the name of husband and wife, and has never had the pleasure of the bedroom, making her great youth wasted in vain. The woman harbored this grievance, and had no one to tell her, causing antipathy to gradually sprout between the couple, which deepened over time. This summer, Xu Jingqing decided to sacrifice her false name in exchange for real benefits, so she hired a lawyer to sue her husband Yao Yanping, saying that she could not bear the abuse, and requested permission to separate and order the defendant to pay alimony of 100,000 yuan. After the first trial of the First Special District Local Court, the plaintiff lost the case. Xu refused to accept it and appealed to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court. After being summoned by the branch court, she was gently persuaded to reconcile. At that time, Xu was unable to insist because of the judge's earnest persuasion, and her hidden feelings were difficult to express, so she had to endure the pain and withdraw the appeal and agree to return to her husband's house to live together. However, she made an angry statement in court, saying that she could not win a lawsuit in the Yangjian court, and she would definitely fight a lawsuit in the Yinjian court in the future. Yao Yanping's mother and his uncle Yao Jinshu heard Xu's angry words and were deeply afraid that Xu would return in the future and cause an unexpected tragedy. Therefore, although Yanping's mother-in-law personally sent her beloved daughter back to the Yao family twice, Yao Jinshu and Yanping's mother refused to accept her, making the mother and daughter travel back and forth in vain. Her antipathy towards Yao Yanping became more and more profound, so she continued to work hard and hired a lawyer to sue Yao Yanping in the First Special Court, requesting an order to perform the obligation of cohabitation, and requesting an order for Yao Jinshu to allow Yanping to live with Xu. Yanping also hired a lawyer to write to the civil mediation office of the court, requesting mediation for divorce because his wife did not respect the elders. Yesterday morning, Judge Yu Changzi opened a court hearing for Xu's lawsuit against Yao. Neither plaintiff nor defendant personally surrendered to the court. After the lawyers from both sides stated their cases, Judge Yu ordered a rescheduling to December 6th at 9:00 am to summon the plaintiff and defendant to court for another hearing.

Page 12

Three Railway Bureaus Announce Resolutions on Improving Shanghai-Beiping Through Train Service 122

The Beijing-Shanghai, Tianjin-Pukou, and Beijing-Ningbo Railway Bureaus, following an order from the Ministry, held a conference on improving the Shanghai-Beiping through train service at the Shanghai North Station from the 14th to the 16th of this month. The resolutions have now been finalized and were announced yesterday morning. A summary is recorded below: (1) Each railway should submit blueprints of the structure and equipment of the through train carriages for reference. Resolution: (A) Passed, exchange blueprints. (B) The standard for carriage equipment should be based on neatness, aesthetics, practicality, and economy. After each railway exchanges blueprints and studies them in detail, the Tianjin-Pukou Railway will convene a meeting to discuss them. (2) The berth numbers should be re-numbered. Resolution: The berth numbers should be numbered by each railway, but each carriage must be different and odd numbers should be for the upper berth and even numbers for the lower berth to avoid misunderstandings. The carriage numbers will remain the same. (3) Third-class carriages should all be equipped with tea rooms. Resolution: The original proposal was amended to "Each passenger train should have a tea room dedicated to providing tea for third-class passengers." (4) Third-class carriages should be equipped with screens and electric fans in the summer to make passengers comfortable. Resolution: (A) Screens will not be installed for the time being. (B) Installation of electric fans is approved in principle and will be studied and implemented by each railway. (5) Third-class sleeper carriages should be operated on the Shanghai-Beiping through train. Resolution: This case has been resolved by the 17th Joint Transportation Conference. After the Ministry issues standard drawings, it will be discussed again. (6) If the carriages of each railway are damaged on other railway sections and affect operation, the railway where the damage occurs should immediately replace them. Resolution: Passed. (7) The uniforms of the conductors in first, second, and third class should be the same for each railway. Resolution: Passed. All will use white long uniforms with no piping and blue and white international numbers embroidered on the left chest from left to right. (8) After the Beijing-Shanghai train of the Shanghai-Beiping through train arrives at Nanjing Station, it is proposed to reduce the number of third-class carriages by one to make it uniform and save power. Resolution: The number of carriages should remain the same as the current method. If charter carriages are used, each railway should negotiate at any time. (9) Standard methods should be specified for adding charter carriages or special passenger carriages to the Shanghai-Beiping through train and the maximum number of carriages to be towed should be determined. Resolution: The latest Ministry order should be followed. The maximum number of carriages to be towed should be limited to twelve. (10) How should the combination of carriages and the order of towing for joint transportation trains be specified to facilitate work and convenience passengers? Resolution: The combination order is specified as follows: (1) Locomotive, (2) Mail car, (3) Third-class car, (4) American sleeper car, (5) Second-class sleeper car, (6) Dining car, (7) First-class sleeper car, (8) Lounge car, (9) Luggage car. In winter or in special circumstances, the Tianjin-Pukou and Beijing-Shanghai Railways should consult temporarily. (11) How should passengers be restricted from carrying items to maintain order? Resolution: Each railway should consider the situation and find ways to crack down on it. (12) How should the order of passengers in first and second class be maintained? Resolution: Each railway should strictly order attendants not to lock rooms with vacant seats and must report to the ticket inspector so that passengers can take their seats. The ticket inspector should be responsible for supervision. (13) When the Shanghai-Beiping through train arrives at major stations, many people picking up passengers enter the train to find them, causing disorder. How should this be restricted to maintain order? Resolution: (A) Passengers getting off the train should be notified of the location of each class of carriage by the ticket inspector. (B) Equipment should be provided on the platform to indicate the location of each class of carriage. (C) People picking up passengers must wait until passengers get off the train before boarding. (14) How should the segmented charging method for tea fees on each train be thoroughly implemented to prevent malfeasance? Resolution: The tea fee is set at two corners per segment (but the Beijing-Shanghai line is set as a small ocean due to special circumstances). It should be collected from passengers all at once, and no other fees should be charged to passengers. (15) Parcel tickets should be issued for the Shanghai-Beiping through train to facilitate passengers. Resolution: The Shanghai-Beiping through train does not handle ordinary parcel transportation. However, passengers carrying typewriters, wireless radios, and instruments may have tickets issued by the transportation department of the departing railway after consideration of the circumstances, and the passenger ticket number should be noted. (16) Improving the method of selling sleeper berths. Resolution: (A) The method of allocating compartments will remain the same, but Tianjin-Pukou will do its best to assist Beijing-Shanghai at any time. (B) The sleeper berth chart should be printed and used according to the format set by the Ministry. (17) When theatrical groups board the Shanghai-Beiping through train, their luggage should be allowed to be transported as baggage. Resolution: The luggage of theatrical groups should not be transported as baggage. However, if it is necessary to carry it with them or in special circumstances, it may be handled in accordance with the parcel ticket resolution. (18) The three points from the Ministry of Railways Joint Transportation Office regarding the improvement of the Shanghai-Beiping through train are proposed for discussion and resolution. Resolution: (A) The dining car is equipped with sand-filtered water, which is very cheap and can be purchased by passengers at any time. There is no need to install a separate sand-filtered water tank. (B) The style of doors and windows should be the same as the Beijing-Shanghai train and soft door curtains should be installed. (C) The urinals of the Beijing-Shanghai train should be improved by the Beijing-Shanghai Railway.

News from the Red Swastika Society's Disaster Relief Efforts 123

The Red Swastika Society is actively carrying out disaster relief efforts in various provinces. The Society's recent work is summarized below.

Hebei and Henan Disaster Relief: The Red Swastika Society previously reported that Changyuan, Puyang, and Hua County in Henan were repeatedly hit by floods, and the situation was serious. It sent special commissioners to provide relief. Now that the severe winter has arrived, the people in the disaster areas have no clothes or food, and the situation awaiting food is even more tragic than before. Another relief team was organized, and President Zhang Zehao was elected as the team leader, leading more than ten staff members and carrying 7,000 yuan in relief funds, 2,000 sets of relief clothing, and relief food and medicines to Changyuan, Puyang, Hua County, and other places to implement relief.

Liyang Disaster Relief: Liyang is the most severely affected area in the Jiangsu Province disaster area. The Southeast Branch of the Red Swastika Society and the Joint Office previously recommended relief commissioners Shi Xiding and Li Tianzhen to investigate the county. The investigation has now been completed and relief tickets have been issued. The first district has 22 townships, with 13,503 large mouths and 15,061 small mouths receiving relief. The second district has 25 townships, with 19,320 large mouths and 17,789 small mouths. The third district has 18 townships, with 17,010 large mouths and 17,675 small mouths. The fourth district has 13 townships, with 18,468 large mouths and 16,694 small mouths. The fifth district has 31 townships, with 26,471 large mouths and 24,439 small mouths. The sixth district has 15 townships, with 6,051 large mouths and 7,844 small mouths. In total, the county has 6 districts and 124 townships, with 100,853 large mouths and 100,502 small mouths. In total, there are 201,355 mouths. The relief standard is 10 catties of noodles for each large mouth and 5 catties of noodles for each small mouth. It is estimated that 37,000 bags of flour are needed, totaling more than 60,000 yuan. In addition to the 35,000 yuan raised by the Red Swastika Society, the Zhiyuan Dharma Assembly, and the Wuxi Puren Charity Association, the Chinese and Foreign Charity Relief Association allocated 15,000 yuan. Mr. Li Shoushan, Song Hanzhang, Lu Bohong, and Gu Jisheng each donated 1,000 yuan. In total, the amount of relief funds raised is still more than 10,000 yuan short.

Haining Disaster Relief: Red Swastika Society relief commissioners Zhao Yulin and Jin Jianguang reported that the investigation of Haining disaster relief is nearing completion, but the drinking water of the people in the disaster area is unclean and many are infected with diseases. They have no money for treatment and most of the able-bodied men have died, which is very pitiful. The society has specially sent Dr. Zhu Xusheng, leading two assistant doctors, carrying various medicines, to set up a temporary clinic for a period of two months. They have already departed on the morning train.

Lihuang Disaster Relief: Zhou Jueci and Jiang Guangji, relief workers from the Red Swastika Society sent to Lihuang, Anhui, reported to the Shanghai General Office by letter, stating that after arriving in Lihuang, they contacted Brigade Commander Zheng and County Chief Xing and other agencies and immediately began an investigation. The county is mostly deserted, and wolves enter the city every night to eat people. More than 20 people have been eaten in the Wang clan ancestral hall refugee shelter. 60 people have been eaten in the fifth district, and 70-80 people have been eaten in the sixth district. More than 100 people whose names are unknown have been eaten by wolves. Most of the refugees are suffering from malaria, and they die after the second onset. The suffering compatriots either die from wolves or from malaria. The tragic situation is heartbreaking.

The seafarer groups, including the Maritime Allied Righteousness Association, the Southern Jun'an Sailors Association, the Yan Ying Southern Society, and the Maritime Helmsman Carpenter Mutual Aid Association, submitted to the Central Executive Committee, etc., stating: Nanjing Central Executive Committee, Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, Ministry of Communications, Greetings. Recently, it was heard that the Song-Han pilot area's pilot management committee violated the purpose of its establishment, favored foreign pilots, and destroyed the few remaining Song-Han pilots. It increased pilotage rates, curbed the development of domestic shipping, and aroused the Shanghai Shipping Association to strike, causing a huge wave that has continued to this day. The Song-Han pilots mostly have experience. If the pilot management committee intends to take back the Tongsha pilotage rights and ban foreign pilots, and hold an examination, it should refer to the situation of national shipping and the experience and ability of each pilot, and test them technically, check their physical condition, and assess their qualifications. They should not be questioned based on the depth of academic theory. Pilotage is very important to national shipping and national defense. If those with superior physical condition, experience, and ability should be guaranteed their jobs in accordance with the law. Even those who are slightly inferior should be given a deadline to remedy their deficiencies and seek ways to make up for their studies in order to cultivate specialized pilot technicians. If senior crew members such as pilots are trampled on, then it will be even more difficult to protect the lower-level crew members such as firemen, sailors, and helmsmen of the Association. The death of the rabbit grieves the fox, and the loss of the lips chills the teeth. The Association telegraphed the Council and Ministries to request that the pilot management committee change the examination method, conduct a re-examination, and not arbitrarily cancel pilot qualifications, destroy Chinese people, and open the door to foreign covetousness. The telegram is full of anticipation.

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted to the Municipal Government yesterday, stating: A presentation for the matter of requesting a presentation, on the 22nd of this month, the Rickshaw Industry Association sent a letter stating, "After reviewing the case, it was found that 64 rickshaw licenses have been in dispute over the issue of leasing. The details have been described and submitted to the Research Association of the Municipal Government on Rickshaw Issues through your Association. Please give it careful handling. After investigating this case, it was found that the dispute was caused by the car merchants Ju Ganxin and Song Fengming, etc., who requested to lease the licenses. The Association invited representatives from both parties to the meeting to discuss the matter, and the method of disposing of the public licenses was resolved. The parties jointly submitted a letter to the Municipal Public Works Bureau, expressing their compliance with the method set by the Association. However, since October, the Municipal Public Works Bureau has withheld this public license for more than a month. The losses of the dozens of poor car merchants who rely on this to make a living are unimaginable, and the number of rickshaw pullers who have lost their jobs as a result has reached more than 300. Their livelihoods are hopeless, and the situation is very pitiful. Although the Association has repeatedly stated the process of resolving the dispute and requested that the livelihoods of the poor be taken into consideration and that the original state be restored, it has not been approved by the Bureau. Recently, the four licenses of Zhang Hengfeng, which were extracted from the 68 magnetic licenses owned by the public in the 17th year of the Republic due to the reduction of the number of cars, will be further withheld. After reviewing the Bureau's handling of this case, it seems to be demanding and has failed to live up to the government's intention to maintain commercial difficulties and help the poor. Recently, it has been heard that the Bureau has suggested to the Municipal Government that it intends to suspend these licenses, which is even more alarming. (Omission) In addition to submitting a request to the Municipal Government to maintain the original state and to issue business permits as soon as possible, the Association has truthfully submitted a request to your Association to submit to the Municipal Government. At the Municipal Government meeting or the Research Association on Rickshaw Issues, when discussing the disposition of these licenses, please allow two representatives from your Association, together with two representatives from the Association, to attend and state the actual truth and the opinions of the car merchants, so as to contribute to the adoption of opinions and avoid misunderstandings, so that the license disputes that affect the business of car merchants and the livelihoods of rickshaw pullers can be handled with caution and satisfaction. The car industry will be very fortunate, etc. The Association found that the Association sent a letter previously, and the Association submitted a request to your Government on October 22 to forward it to the Research Committee on Rickshaw Issues for careful handling. So far, no reply has been received. According to the news obtained by the Association, the Public Works Bureau insists on canceling these licenses, which makes the business situation even more precarious. It is believed that if these car licenses are, as proposed by the Association, rented to poor car households by the Association and the rent is allocated to the educational expenses of the industry, it will be of benefit to the poor car households and will also take care of the educational foundation of the industry. It does not seem to conflict with the Municipal Government and the Public Works Bureau's main purpose of maintaining public welfare. According to the previous letter, it is appropriate to prepare a document to submit to your Government for review. It is hoped that when the Research Committee on Rickshaw Issues discusses the method of handling these car licenses, the Association will be allowed to send two representatives to attend and state their contributions, so as to use the small efforts for adoption. It is really for the public's convenience, etc.

General Assembly of the French Concession Boiled Water Shop Trade Association 130

Discussing the French Police's Obstruction of the Association's Organization

Resolving to Issue a Declaration and Send Representatives to Petition

There are a total of 280 boiled water shops in the French Concession. Although there is a trade association, many have not joined, leading to disorderly business practices and a lack of uniformity. Therefore, Dong Wenwei and other members of the trade initiated the establishment of the Second Special District Office of the Shanghai Boiled Water Shop Trade Association. The trade association appointed Dong Wenli as the director of the office, and the application was submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for approval and filing. It was also permitted to be established by the French Consul General. Since the office began its operations, all members of the trade have enthusiastically joined, and it was declared established last month. After the establishment, all members of the trade agreed to abide by the trade regulations, and the office supervised the production of water ladles to be distributed to the members and stipulated a unified water price method, which was scheduled to be implemented on a specific date. However, the French police, due to a misunderstanding regarding the distribution of water ladles and the unified water price, prevented the distribution and ordered the office to be closed. Upon hearing the news, all members of the trade were extremely indignant. Therefore, at 2 PM yesterday, an emergency meeting of all members of the trade was held at the Zizhu Temple on Zhaozhou Road in the Chinese territory. More than 110 members of the trade attended. The trade association appointed Standing Committee member Li Shengxian, representatives of the First Special District Office Sheng Jinggui, Wang Zhitian, Fang Guangwen, etc., to attend and provide guidance. After the formalities were completed, Li Shengxian was publicly elected as the chairman, and Dong Wenli reported on the entire process. The following measures were decided upon: (1) Fifteen people, including Ji Zihe, Chen Bingnan, Dong Wenli, and Cheng Peizhang, were nominated as representatives to petition various party and government agencies on a regular basis, requesting them to negotiate with the French authorities. (2) A request was submitted to the trade association to forward it to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for negotiation. (3) Pending a resolution, the office would be temporarily set up inside the Zizhu Temple. (4) The reasons for the French authorities' revocation of the organization were investigated, citing oppression of the trade. In addition to the trade association negotiating on the basis of reason, the representatives would also jointly declare to the French authorities that there was no oppression and request restoration. (5) Reorganizing business operations was a matter for the trade itself and had nothing to do with public order. Since it did not violate the law, nor was there any oppressive behavior, a declaration should be issued, asking all industries to uphold justice and provide sympathetic assistance. (6) The office would notify members of the trade to bring their seals to the association to collect the water ladles. (7) The issue of unified water prices would be notified again and implemented on a specific date after the water ladles were distributed. (8) The various handling processes would be reported to the trade association for forwarding to the relevant party and government agencies for filing. (9) If the above measures were interfered with by foreigners and could not be implemented, it was decided that all would express their determination to sacrifice everything. (10) A fee of one yuan was stipulated for the water ladle and one yuan for maintenance, with membership fees to be collected after the water price was unified. The meeting adjourned after the resolutions were passed.

An Apprentice Carrying Money Was Robbed, and a Policeman Arrested a Thief 137

A Stray Bullet Wounds a Female Pedestrian

Xu Qisheng, a 19-year-old apprentice from Yong Sheng Chang tobacco and paper shop at 177 Huanghe Road in the French Concession, went to Wanxing Money Exchange on Avenue Paul Beau yesterday afternoon with 200 yuan to exchange for banknotes. After the exchange, on his way back, when he passed the intersection of Rue Chapsal and Rue Aiguebelle, two robbers suddenly jumped out from the side of the road, blocked his way, and threatened him with a gun, robbing him of all the banknotes in his possession. After obtaining the loot, the robbers fled into the Chinese territory of Fangbang Road via Nanyang Bridge. After being robbed, Xu was unwilling to give in and desperately chased after them, shouting loudly for help. The robbers, seeing Xu chasing closely, became angry and fired a shot behind them. A stray bullet accidentally hit a pedestrian in the leg. At this time, the police from both the Chinese and French territories heard the alarm and surrounded the area. Seeing that the situation was not good, the robbers threw their guns on Fangbang Road. At this time, the Chinese police had already chased after them with guns and arrested one of the robbers on the spot, taking him to the Ximen Branch for detention. According to the confession, his name is Liu Liansheng, from Qingjiang, and he is 28 years old. He admitted to the robbery without hesitation. The injured woman was taken to the hospital for treatment by the police.

Firecrackers Explode, Injuring Three People 138

A Rickshaw is Destroyed

Kong Linbo, a 31-year-old man from Taixing, has been running Hua Yuan firecracker workshop at 58 Puyudong Road outside the Dananmen in the South City. His business was usually doing well. Yesterday afternoon, around 1 PM, Kong handed over two large boxes of firecrackers to his partners, Xing Junlu and Gu Zhenping, to be moved to the front of the store, and hired Li Jiongming (22 years old), a Hainanese rickshaw puller, to transport them to western Shanghai for sale. Unexpectedly, when Xing Junlu and others were carrying the two boxes of firecrackers onto the rickshaw, the rickshaw toppled because of the unstable arrangement. More than 8,000 firecrackers inside the boxes exploded with a loud bang. At the same time, the rickshaw was instantly destroyed, and the rickshaw puller Li Jiongming and Xing Junlu, Gu Zhenping and other three people standing next to the rickshaw, their heads and faces were severely injured by the explosion. In an instant, they were covered in blood and screamed in agony. The police officer Zhang Yukun from the Xun Dao Street Police Station in charge of the area rushed to the scene upon hearing the news. In addition to sending Li and others to Shanghai Hospital for treatment, he took Kong Linbo, the owner of the Hua Chang firecracker workshop, to the station. After questioning by Director Jin, he was ordered to be detained for investigation and handling.

Memorial Service for Mr. Wang Zhenzhi Held by Various Guangdong Organizations 139

Mr. Wang Zhenzhi, a famous Cantonese official and the father of lawyer Wang Siji, was kind and gentle, and treated people with loyalty and forgiveness. In the early years of the Republic, he served as the Chief of Civil Affairs of Panyu County, Guangdong Province, where he achieved remarkable political achievements. After leaving office, he went to Shantou to take up the position of Superintendent of the Chao Hai Customs and Section Chief of the Commissioner for Foreign Affairs, where he was highly respected. Because of his expertise in law, his integrity, his diplomatic skills, and his diligence in his duties, the consuls of various countries stationed in Shantou respected and feared him. In 1927, he retired due to old age. The National Government, in recognition of his contributions, granted him a lifetime pension, making him one of the few who were specially awarded such an honor. Unfortunately, he passed away at his residence in Shantou on the 9th of last month. Upon hearing the sad news, many people expressed their regret. Recently, lawyer Wang returned to Shanghai after handling the funeral. The Shanghai branch of the Lian Yi Association, the board of directors of the Weixing Girls' School, the Gonghe Le Sports Association, the Cantonese Lawyers' Association, the Alumni Association of the Schools for Officials' Dependents in Guangdong, and the Panyu Guildhall and other colleagues jointly initiated a memorial service to express their condolences. It was specifically scheduled for the 25th of this month at the Yushan Hall on Xin Guangdong Street, Zhabei, as the memorial venue. In recent days, the presentation of memorial scrolls and elegiac couplets has been extremely grand, and important party and government figures have all made donations.

Publication of the "Nanjing City Special Issue" of the "China Economic Records" 140

Since Nanjing became the capital of the National Government, it has become the political center of the country, and its transportation, culture, economy, etc. have all advanced rapidly, and the changes in the economic situation have been even more dramatic. However, those who are enthusiastic about studying the capital's economy often suffer from the lack of good books as a basis for reference. The Economic Survey Institute of the Construction Committee, seeing this, sent personnel to conduct a detailed survey, and then carefully compiled and statistically analyzed the obtained materials. After spending two months, the entire book has been edited and completed, and was published and distributed yesterday. The content of the book is divided into chapters on land, population, municipal administration, transportation, industry and commerce, finance, etc. It covers everything about Nanjing's mountains, cultural relics, customs, and economy. With this book in hand, one not only feels like personally visiting the capital, taking in all the famous scenic spots and the great new buildings, but also clearly understands all the changes that have taken place in Nanjing in recent years. The sales outlets in this city are the Zuo Zhe Book Society on the Fourth Road, and the Modern Bookstore, at four silver dollars per copy.

Establishment of the Old Timber Trade Association 141

The Old Timber Trade Association held its founding meeting at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce the other day. More than one hundred members attended. Zhu Yakui from the Municipal Party Department, Zhang Dafu from the Social Affairs Bureau, and Li Ruzhang from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce attended the meeting to provide guidance. Chen Chunyang and Ling Yongde were publicly elected as temporary chairmen. First, the chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting and the preparations made. Representatives from party and government agencies then gave speeches. Then, the articles of association were adopted, and the executive committee members were elected. As a result, Chen Chunyang, Fan Genchu, Ling Yongde, Chen Xianshen, Zhou Xinbao, Zhang Mingcai, Lu Yuncheng, Chen Baochu, Zhao Wenyuan, Fang Fayu, Yu Shuping, Liu Zhenshan, Chen Eqing, Liu Suilin, and Jiang Fangzhou were elected as executive committee members. Xu Xianglin, Xu Qinglai, and Le Fulin were alternate executive committee members. They were sworn in on the spot. Subsequently, several motions were discussed, and a group photo was taken to commemorate the occasion. The association convened its first executive committee meeting yesterday and mutually elected Chen Chunyang, Ling Yongde, Chen Xianshen, Fan Genchu, and Liu Suilin as standing committee members. Chen Chunyang was also elected as the chairman.

Spring and Autumn

Little West Heaven 144

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Five: Fawning and Flattering with a Lamp to Illuminate a Withered Face, Driven by a Hungry Stomach, Applying Powder to Learn Debauchery

He was still hating him, but he didn't expect him to come to apologize first, so he also had a smile. In fact, Jia Duocai was a misunderstanding. He thought that Li Shilian had invited him on time because Zhu Yueying had come. When he arrived at the courtyard gate and saw Hu Saozi here again, he was even happier. In his excitement, he said that sentence to compliment Hu Saozi. He didn't expect that when he walked into Li Shilian's house, it was unexpected. Zhang Jiefu and Guo Dunpin were both here, especially with a woman in her twenties. In Xi'an, although this woman was very gorgeous, the powder on her cheeks was a little sticky, and the faint blue lines under her eyes were obviously unable to hide her haggardness. She seemed to know that Jia Duocai was a spender. Therefore, as soon as Jia Duocai entered the door, she stood up first, smiling to greet him. Jia Duocai was staring at her blankly when Li Shilian rushed forward and said: "Let me introduce you, this is Mr. Jia, this is Miss Yang, her courtesy name is Huanhua, friends call her Miss Wu, we also call her Miss Wu. She's also our fellow villager." Jia Duocai estimated her, originally thinking she was a woman of the streets, but now listening to Li Shilian's tone of introduction, it didn't seem like it, so he didn't dare to despise her too much, nodded and smiled: "Miss Wu is indeed our fellow villager, rare, which county?" Huanhua glanced at Guo Dunpin, then smiled and said the two words Changshu. Jia Duocai smiled: "That's even more coincidental, and it's the same county. But Miss Wu's accent has changed a bit, I think she's been away from her hometown for many years." Huanhua said: "I went to Shanghai at the age of nine, this year I left my hometown..." She said this, unwilling to say it in one breath, pondered for a long time with her head slightly tilted, and then smiled: "It's also been more than nine years." Li Shilian smiled at her: "Two nines are eighteen, is Miss Wu eighteen years old this year?" (72)

Golden Wonton Noodle Stand 145

— Qing Qu

I once heard an old saying from the elders: There was a poor scholar who suffered a great tragedy in his childhood. He relied on his mother's chastity and upbringing to grow up. Later, he made progress and was able to hold a prominent position. However, when he was young, when he thought of his mother, enduring hardship and suffering, even in the deep of night, she was still rocking the spinning wheel with one hand and pulling the yarn with the other, spinning the yarn into skeins, accumulating enough to weave cloth, and then changing to another job. Therefore, his loud reading voice was often accompanied by the continuous sound of the yarn on his mother's spinning wheel. Even the neighbors heard this hard-working situation and said in their sleep, "Alas! This virtuous mother and good son, although they are suffering now, will definitely have a turnaround one day!" Later, he thought of his reading success as being due to his mother's spinning and reading with him under the lamp when he was young. Therefore, after he achieved his ambition, he imitated and made a small cart, which he placed in his ancestral hall as a permanent memorial. This is a story from my hometown. Also, in Shanghai, like it's Sipailou! There was a Mr. Chen who, it is said, initially carried a coppersmith's stand, but later he became rich and became a wealthy man. Therefore, his descendants could not bear to forget the original business of their ancestors, so they also made a very small coppersmith's stand and placed it in their ancestral hall. These are all rare and special souvenirs that were rarely heard of before. Hey! Yesterday, I was sipping tea at Tayin and heard my old friend Wang Wangnong say: There is a wonton seller in Jiangwan, but I don't know his name. He carries this stand every day, comes out in the afternoon, and doesn't go back until late at night. It is because the goods he brings in every day must be sold out before he can make a living. Unexpectedly, he worked hard and his business was not bad. Over time, he became a well-off family. Later, he changed to running a flour mill. He encountered opportunities for the rise and fall of flour prices. It can be said that when the time comes, everything goes well. In a few years, he became a wealthy man. Therefore, if you go to this town and ask, not only is his gate tall and big, but in his ancestral hall, there is also a wonton stand made of pure gold, and there are pots, firewood, bowls, and ladles, and the drawers are arranged in layers, everything is available. Therefore, I have recorded it so that we can see that there is no big or small occupation. If you can do it with perseverance and perseverance, you can accumulate wealth and become rich.

Flower Village 147

— Sheng Xiaoli

Flower Village, what a beautiful and poetic name this is. In everyone's ideal, it must be a "land of bliss," a "Shangri-La," or the villas of wealthy gentlemen. But in reality, it is not entirely so, or rather, there is a more heartbreaking page to it. Let me briefly describe it: Flower Village is located in Zhabei Pengpu Zhao's Garden, with more than 400 households, mostly engaged in the flower industry. The village is surrounded by flower fields and greenhouses, indeed a naturally secluded environment. This autumn, Mr. Huang Jingwan established a school there, designated as a rural education experimental zone, dedicated to improving the lives of farmers, experimenting with the education of "flowers." For the past two months, during our work breaks, we have often strolled through the fields, greenhouses, vegetable gardens, bamboo fences, and thatched huts; almost everywhere has our footprints. The farmers and their wives, laughing and chatting, have an unspeakable joy! We have gained a lot of information from approaching the farmers. The other day, I met a farmer friend who said, "I have been growing flowers for forty years, and every year it's always difficult to make ends meet, it's really hard!" I was surprised and asked him, "Why is that?" He said, "Most of our flowers are sold to foreigners, and even the seeds are imported from abroad. We buy the seeds at a very high price, and the price of the flowers is entirely determined by the foreigners. If the price is too high, the flowers won't sell." After hearing these words, I couldn't help but feel touched. Flower Village is truly a place for foreigners to plant flowers. The farmers are indirectly working as second-class foreign slaves. The flowers of Flower Village do not belong to the people of Flower Village, but to the foreigners. Flower Village has living flowers, but no right to enjoy them with a full stomach. Being so close to the Shanghai flower district, their lives are in the hands of foreigners. Alas, what else can be said!

The Contest for the Championship 148

Records of Incense Drifting and Fading 149

— Original by Princess Deling of Qing, translated by Qin Shouou

I was secretly wondering: up to this point, had the Empress Dowager felt the sadness of this desolate and melancholic scene that was unfolding here? Or perhaps she felt it, but was just enduring it, unwilling to show anything; or perhaps this feeling had not even registered on her nerves! Because no matter how healthy she was, her age was, after all, advanced, and older people's senses are not usually very sharp; plus, she was very tired today, so she would naturally be even more dull. But I was still a young person, and a particularly imaginative young person.

Because I was so good at imagining, my emotions were easily moved. Seeing this desolate and melancholic night scene at this moment, I couldn't help but regret that I shouldn't have followed the imperial entourage to the east, and I had a strong desire to return to Beijing immediately. However, I also understood my own nature very well; although this desire had arisen, it was only a fleeting impulse after being stimulated on a nerve, and it would never turn into a passionate demand; maybe after a night's sleep, I wouldn't think like this anymore tomorrow!

But no matter what, I couldn't force myself to be brave. It was like a child who had a terrible nightmare in bed; even after waking up, they would be so scared that they would cry. Now that such a ghostly hallucination had arisen in my nerves, it seemed as if there were many ghostly shadows, coming and going hazily in this vast and dimly lit ancient palace. And I kept explaining to myself: "It's true! There must be ghosts here! Just like there must be ghosts in the Imperial Palace in Beijing. In these two palace courtyards, over thousands or hundreds of years, who knows how many people have died inside; although their corpses have been transported out for burial, their souls will remain forever." (182)

Another Defense of Asparagus 150

— (Bu Gu)

A few days ago, I read Mr. Nangongsheng's writing about asparagus in this publication, and I felt quite doubtful. Later, I read Fu Fusheng's defense, and I breathed a sigh of relief, but there is still a misunderstanding, so I might as well write it out for everyone to discuss.

As far as I know, asparagus is planted by dividing the roots. The stems grow in clumps, and the thin leaves are very similar to dill. The shoots are the tender buds of the plant in the soil. It is not guaranteed that they can be harvested after planting for a few months; it takes about a year or more. The method of cultivation is roughly the same as our cultivation of chives, but we don't bury the whole plant, we only raise the soil around the roots from time to time.

There is an agriculturist in Hangzhou, Mr. Tang, who has grown asparagus, which shows that this thing can also be grown domestically. Don't think that this is just an imported product and let it be imported every year! I hope that those who aspire to save the country through agriculture will pay attention to it.

Notice: It is hereby announced that, according to a letter from Mr. Huo Xueming, the "Dragon Cave Transformation in Jinhua" by the Qixia Tower Master in the "Autumn Excursion Special Issue" of the 10th is plagiarized from his old work "Going to Shuanglong Cave" from April. This kind of despicable behavior is extremely hateful. In addition to canceling his remuneration, this is specially announced.

Places Visited

Two Days of Travel Notes in Beijing 151

— Yinqiu

Nanjing is originally a place I have visited before. My first acquaintance with it was more than fifteen years ago, when I was a student taking entrance exams, full of ambition. After taking office, before the provincial capital was moved to Zhenjiang, I went to Beijing at least two or three times a year due to serving in social education and attending meetings for discussions. However, I have not visited in the past three years. This time, as a representative of the Suzhou Provincial Library, I went to Beijing to attend the joint meeting of vocational education teachers from provincial social education institutions. I had the opportunity to visit this old place and stay for two nights. It happened to be windy and rainy, and I came and went in a hurry. I only managed to compose ten short poems, playfully using the original rhymes of the Tang people, to record my feelings about the mud and snow!

First: Boarding the bus and meeting Zhi, using Zhang Yue's rhyme from "Late Period on the Shu Road." "Meeting an old friend on the bus, asking each other about the journey, you are heading to Liangxi, I am coming to Baixia City." November 11th, it happened to be Sunday. When taking the express train around 9 o'clock, there were more than 200 members of the Nanjing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo special party department visiting the mausoleum, and many tourists going to Yixing to explore the Shanjuan and Gengsang Caves. The car was extremely crowded. As soon as the car started, I suddenly saw Mr. Zhu Lezhou, the principal of the Zhongshan Physical Education School. He got off the bus in Wuxi, and we only asked each other about our journey.

Second: Looking at the distant mountains from the car, using Li Bai's rhyme from "Autumn Pu Song." "The fog gradually clears, the car travels unknowingly for a long time, distant mountains send off outside the window, red leaves are drunk and congealed with frost." When the car started, the clouds and fog were hazy, and the shadow of the Tiger Hill Pagoda was almost indistinguishable. It wasn't until Wuxi that the clouds gradually dispersed and the fog cleared, and the green mountains and red trees sent off the car window, which was a delight.

Third: Arriving in Beijing and lodging at Shushixuan, using Dai Shulun's rhyme from "Sanlv Temple." "The guesthouse is so refined and elegant, quietly hidden deep in a winding path, the small pavilion is inscribed 'Shushixuan', the garden is full of late chrysanthemums." From Xiaguan into the city, all are flat avenues. The car passed by many new buildings on both sides, splendid and magnificent, with a majestic atmosphere, like celestial palaces. Post offices and banks have all become towering buildings. The prosperity of the market around Sixiang Bridge is no longer what it used to be. The guesthouse is located in the Jiaotong Hotel on Zhongzheng Street, quiet in the midst of the hustle and bustle, and the location is quite elegant. In the garden, there is Shushixuan, the pond water ripples, and the chrysanthemum bushes are in full bloom, which is quite interesting.

Fourth: Night rain, using Wei Yingwu's rhyme from "Autumn Night Sending to Qiu Yuanwai." "The hotel is quiet late at night, just in time for a light rain, many green bamboos in front of the window, rustling and unable to sleep." Because tomorrow is the Prime Minister's birthday, there are many members of the mausoleum visit group in the hotel. There are many people and noises, and it is quiet late at night. Just as I was thinking of falling asleep, the sound of rain on the bamboo window was rustling. The traveler heard this and could not fall asleep.

Fifth: Going to the meeting, passing through Gongyuan Road, using Linghu Chu's rhyme from "Thinking of You." "Long time no see Gongyuan Road, many feelings of vicissitudes, the most unforgettable old event, once spent with the old man." On the 12th, braving the rain, I went to the Nanjing People's Education Center on Gongyuan Road, which is the meeting place. The roads along the way were being rebuilt, and the car drove around. When I arrived, I learned that most of the old friends in the meeting were scattered, and most of what I saw were new acquaintances. Recalling that I had twice accompanied the old Mr. Tao Xiaozhi to this place in the past, but he has already returned to Daoshan, I can't help but feel sad!

Sixth: After the meeting, going to a banquet at a restaurant, using Li Shizhi's rhyme from "Resigning as Prime Minister." "The virtuous gather with joy, the successful meeting shares a cup, the guests at the top of the windy and rainy building, mostly come from afar." On this day, during the meeting, the implementation of social education was discussed in great detail. After the meeting, the colleagues from the Nanjing People's Education Center publicly hosted the representatives from various institutions at a restaurant in front of the Confucius Temple. Among the guests, there were those from Nantong, Qingjiang, and other places, and the toasting and clinking of cups were quite a grand occasion for a time.

Seventh: Sitting in the rain by the guest window, using Qian Qi's rhyme from "Looking at Mount Lu from the River." Originally agreed to go with Sun Lu, but the muddy road cannot be climbed, listening to the rain by the guest window for a long time, sitting silently as a monk. Originally agreed that after the meeting, taking advantage of the Prime Minister's birthday, we would go together to respectfully visit the tomb; but because the rain did not stop, the road was muddy, and the stone steps on the tomb were high and steep, slippery and difficult to support, so it did not work out as desired, and it had to be left for another day.

Eighth: Gazing alone at the Qinhuai River, using Wei Yingwu's rhyme from "Answering Li Huan." "Making each other for not many days, happy to steal leisure from busyness, the new Qinhuai River rises green, tired birds want to fly back." In the evening, the rain stopped, and I strolled around Zhuque Road and Wuyi Lane. The scenery was as before, but the road administration was much better. I went to the small park on the Qinhuai River and saw that the lake water had risen green, and there was no longer the drought of the past. I bought a few kinds of food, preparing to return quickly tomorrow, because the thought of returning home was already urgent.

Ninth: Setting off early on the way home, using Luo Binwang's rhyme from "Farewell at Yishui." "Waking up from a dream, the sky is just dawning, putting on clothes and straightening my hat, few passengers boarding the car, the morning breeze is cold all the way." I got up at dawn, but the rain had not stopped. In the hazy sky, I took a car to Xiaguan. The car traveled very fast, and the morning breeze was very cold. The sky may be expected to clear up.

Tenth: Arriving home, using Cen Shen's rhyme from "Thinking of Chang'an Hometown on the Ninth Day of Military Service." "Don't say the journey is short, I left and returned in a hurry, arriving home as if after a long separation, my wife and children greet me with smiling faces." The car passed Zhenjiang, and the sky gradually cleared. When I arrived in Suzhou, the sun was shining brightly. Entering the city and arriving home, it was only past noon. Although it was only a short separation, my wife and children greeted me at the door, and the whole family spoke happily, like a distant guest returning home for the first time.
