Sports News

Public Race Walking to Be Held Tomorrow Morning 152

Starting at 8:00 AM at Jing'an Temple Road and Tongfu Road

A Total of 117 Male and Female Athletes from Four Groups

Women's Race Walking Scheduled for 11:00 AM at Shen Garden

The 4th public race walking event organized by the Chinese Race Walking Association (the 3rd for women) has been widely praised by all sectors since its preparation, and has been guided and assisted by the Sports Association, which has enabled it to proceed smoothly. The entire route has been slightly changed. The men's race has been increased to 13 miles and 800 meters, and the women's race is 1.5 miles. It has been scheduled to be held at 8:00 AM and 11:00 AM tomorrow morning, respectively, rain or shine. 117 men and women have registered to participate, including 78 men, from the Morning Light, San Duo, Meteor, and Navy, Army, and Air Force teams. There are 39 women. Although fewer people are participating in this competition than in previous years, they are well-trained and strong. The fierce competition and crowded audience at that time will definitely cause a sensation in Shanghai. Details are as follows:

Full Route: Male competitors must gather at the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Tongfu Road at 7:30 AM tomorrow morning, sign in at 7:30 AM, line up at 7:50 AM, and start at 8:00 AM. All clothes will be handed over to the escorts to carry in the car to prevent the racers from getting cold. The route goes along Jing'an Temple Road, Jessfield Road, to Wujiaochang, then enters Baidian Road, crosses the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, to Zhoujiaqiao, turns into Hobilan Road (i.e., Hualun Road, Hongqiao Road), passes through Haige Road, goes straight into Tyssdall Road, turns into Yao Bishop Road, Avenue Petain, Avenue Joffre, Avenue du Roi Albert, crosses Avenue Foch, to Seymour Road, turns into Xinzha Road, Jiaozhou Road, Connaught Road, to Taiping Road, goes straight into the Shen Garden track and field, and then runs one lap around the track to stop, for a total of 13 miles and 800 meters. The women's competition will be held on the Shen Garden track and field, running six laps around the track, for a total of 1.5 miles. Participants must arrive at the venue at 10:45 AM, sign in at 10:50 AM, and start the race at 11:00 AM, with awards presented at 11:30 AM.

Joining Sections: The introducers are very important for the progress of the race walkers during the competition. Therefore, each competitor is allowed to invite one introducer to accompany them. However, due to the large number of participants, the introducers have to join in sections. Racers numbered 1 to 30 should wait at the intersection of Brenan Road and Yuyuan Road (i.e., in front of the entrance of Zhaofeng Garden) and join the introduction. Racers numbered 31 to 78 can only join the introduction at the intersection of Brenan Road and Jessfield Road (i.e., Wujiaochang). However, they must all withdraw at Jiaozhou Road and take a small road straight into the north gate of Shen Garden. The association has specially recorded the regulations that competitors and introducers must know during the competition as follows:

Competitor's Notes: (1) Competitors must proceed on the designated avenue and are not allowed to step onto the sidewalk. (2) When a competitor overtakes a competitor in front, they must maintain a distance of three steps to the left or right before proceeding. The competitor in front is not allowed to deliberately obstruct. (3) If a competitor has other reasons during the competition, they are allowed to leave the designated road, but must return to the original place before proceeding. (4) Competitors must stand straight with their chests out, swing their arms freely, look straight ahead, and use their heels and toes when striding. However, the heel of the front foot must not touch the ground until the toe of the rear foot is lifted, and the knee must be straight when the front foot touches the ground (i.e., must be straight when the rear foot is lifted). (5) If a competitor violates the above rules, the course referee will report to the chief referee for a warning or disqualification.

Introducer's Notes: (1) Start joining the introduction and withdrawing at the designated location. (2) May ride a bicycle or walk. (3) The introducer must not follow anyone other than the designated competitor. (4) Except for providing food and drink to the competitor, they are not allowed to touch the competitor. (5) When a competitor behind is overtaking, the introducer in front must not deliberately obstruct. (6) If an introducer violates the above rules, they will also be warned by the course referee or disqualified.

This Year's Winter Vacation Physical Education Teacher Training Examination Held by the Ministry of Education 155

Academic and Practical Exams

The Ministry of Education noted that while middle schools, such as regular senior and junior high schools, and normal schools have all held unified exams, physical education schools have not. Therefore, it has decided to hold a unified examination for physical education schools during this year's winter vacation. However, there are only a few physical education middle schools, mostly physical education normal schools with only senior high school level. Therefore, instead of calling it a physical education school unified exam, it is better to call it a physical education normal school unified exam (mostly senior high school level, with no junior high school level specialized schools). The subjects for this unified exam are different from those for regular middle schools. Regular middle schools only test academic subjects, while this physical education unified exam places equal emphasis on both academic and practical subjects. In addition to testing major academic subjects, practical skills such as track and field events and ball games must also be tested. The standards for the academic and practical exams are currently being discussed by the Director of General Education and the Physical Education Inspector. Once the standards are set, they will be announced and implemented.

Education News

Anhui Provincial Education Inspection Group Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 160

Led by Yang Lian, the group visited the city center in the afternoon

An Anhui Provincial Domestic Education Inspection Group of forty people, led by Yang Lian, Director of the Anhui Education Department, arrived in Shanghai from Hangzhou yesterday afternoon. They are staying at the Oriental Hotel and plan to inspect Shanghai for four days before heading north. The details are recorded below.

Purpose of the Inspection In recent years, secondary education in the province has gradually reached a reasonable level. However, local education in various counties has no foundation to speak of. In recent years, floods and droughts have occurred frequently and without end. After the abolition of exorbitant taxes, there is no way to compensate for education funding, so that local education is almost bankrupt. The Anhui Provincial Department of Education plans to convene a local education administrative conference in December to deal with the current difficult problems in local education and to open up new ways for future improvement. Before the meeting, a domestic education inspection group will be organized to conduct on-site inspections in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Shandong, Hebei, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces to learn from each other. The purpose of the inspection is: (1) To inspect new facilities and new methods in domestic local education as a reference for improving local education in the province; (2) To discuss with education experts from other provinces issues such as "how to properly select talent and methods," "how to compensate and broadly raise local education funding after the abolition of exorbitant taxes," and "how to integrate elementary education and social education and assist rural production" in the hope of obtaining appropriate solutions; (3) Based on the findings of the inspection, to study and implement the easiest, most economical, and most effective methods of promoting universal education, and to plan new ways for local education in the province.

Organization of the Entire Group The group is organized by Director Yang of the Education Department, leading principals of provincial normal schools, heads of provincial social education institutions, heads of local education, principals of elementary schools, and staff of the Education Department. The names are as follows (Leader) Yang (Members) Wang Dexi, Wang Jiayou, Wang Shulan, Fang Ming, Fang Yisheng, Jiang Xun, Wang Dequan, Shen Weixia, Shen Zixiu, Song Zhentao, Li Weitang, Li Daliao, Wu Wanzeng, Zhou De, Zhou Xueying, Zhou Huazhen, Jin Hui, Duan Zeyi, Hu Jiajian, Hu Heng, Tang Jie, Gao Chaozong, Ni Zide, Chen Dongyuan, Chen Diyong, Xia Zongyu, Xu Ningsheng, Cheng Mian, Shu Dejin, Xi Guoguang, Huang Lunshu, Huang Daolin, Zhang Dezheng, Zhang Fazhou, Yang Zizhen, Ye Weizhen, Ye Kunfu, Deng Shao, Liu Huaiyu, Tan Hegao.

Arrival in Shanghai The inspection group arrived in Shanghai at 1:00 PM yesterday afternoon. After all the members of the group got off the train, they went to the Oriental Hotel on Tibet Road to rest.

Visiting the City The entire group had lunch and then, guided by Huang Jingwan and Xu Jian, visited various new constructions of the Greater Shanghai Plan in the city center. They first went to the Municipal Government for a week of visits, and then to the Education Bureau. Director Pan of the Education Bureau happened to be in Beijing on official business, and the head of the School Education Section, Chen Bai, represented him in receiving the group and reported in detail on the actual situation of education in Shanghai.

During the banquet, the chairman, Wang Yunwu, first gave a welcome speech, followed by Yang Lian, the leader of the group, who gave a thank-you speech and briefly described the progress of education in Anhui Province and the origins and purposes of organizing the education inspection group to visit various provinces. Subsequently, Cai Yuanpei, Huang Renzhi, Tao Xingzhi, Jiang Wenyu, Tai Shuangqiu, Dai Jiqian, and Zong Rong successively gave speeches, elaborating on the promotion of universal education, the raising of local education funds, and the socialization of school education, making it a rare grand event in the academic circles of Shanghai. At 9:30 PM, the guests and hosts dispersed in joy.

Today's Itinerary It is said that the group is scheduled to visit the Shanhai Institute of Technology at 8:00 AM today, go to Zhabei to pay respects to the war dead in the afternoon, and the China Bookstore will host a banquet at the New Asia Restaurant in the evening.

(3) The inspections in various places have provided many lessons for solving the educational problems in the province and have been very helpful. Shenbao Radio Weekly

The Installation of Radio Transceivers on Airplanes 167

— Zhenmin

In recent years, the use of radios on airplanes has been increasing daily. This is undoubtedly a bright page in the history of radio, and it is well worth our attention and research. I will briefly describe the latest installation methods below, which I think readers will also be happy to hear.

(1) Radio Equipment Used on Airplanes

The various radio equipment used on airplanes is not much different from that used on land. The only difference is the design issue, which makes it suitable for the special conditions of aviation. The most important thing is that the equipment must be extremely light in weight, and at the same time, the volume occupied must be extremely small, so that the airplane can carry it without difficulty. The structure of each part of the equipment must be extremely strong, so that it will not change shape even after the strong vibration of the airplane during driving. Therefore, each moving part should be absolutely locked in its position after being adjusted once. The base of the vacuum tube must be made of soft sponge-like rubber, and the radio box should also be placed on a cushion that is rich in vibration absorption, so as to minimize violent vibrations.

In addition to the above points, there is one most important point, that is, under no circumstances can sparks occur in any circuit, because the wings of the airplane are all coated with oilcloth or flammable paint. When the engine is started, there is often vaporized gasoline, which can cause the entire airplane to explode or burn when it touches a spark. Therefore, the exterior of all circuits should be wrapped with strong insulation, and all circuits should be tightly connected to the wooden frame of the fuselage to prevent vibration. All switches should be specially made to isolate the outside air (such as using a shell, etc.).

All circuits used on land can be applied to airplanes. However, the application of storage batteries is quite difficult, because the charging problem is difficult to carry out during the continuous driving of the airplane. Using a very small generator to obtain electrical energy has now proven to have very good results. This type of generator can be installed on the wings or behind the propeller. The air pressure generated when the fuselage moves forward is used to drive the small fan on the generator to generate friction electricity. The current generated can be adjusted by special vacuum tubes and resistors to maintain a constant transmission.

(2) Antenna Installation and Sound Reception and Transmission

There are about two types of antennas used for airplane radio, namely (1) "Loop Antenna" and (2) "Open Antenna." "Loop Antenna" is commonly used on land and is quite suitable for short-wave transmission and reception. As for "Open Antenna," it is more widely used. The diagram is as follows:

This type of antenna is made of bare wire 300 feet long. One end is tied to the antenna shaft on the fuselage, and the other end is tied to a small lead block to make it float in the air. This antenna is led out of the airplane through a guide tube (as shown in Figure 1). The interior of the guide tube is a metal surface that is in direct contact with the antenna and leads to the radio box to connect the circuit. The length of the antenna can be adjusted with a rotating shaft (the antenna needs to be shortened when the airplane lands to avoid breaking).

Because the weight of the falling lead block often causes the airplane to lose its balance, the remedy is to add appropriate balancing objects to the engine part. The broadcasting effect of the radio waves can be seen in (Figure 2). Because the antenna is installed unbalanced, the electric axis is often moved, so the highest radio wave transmission and reception is often slightly to the right of the fuselage. This is what the driver should pay attention to.

The cross-sectional view of the guide tube can be viewed in detail in (Figure 3). The outer tube is made of Bakelite or other insulating material and is tightly installed on the side of the fuselage. The inner tube is made of metal, and the antenna passes through this tube. There is a wiring terminal next to the inner tube to connect to the electric box.

The length of the antenna varies with the wavelength. In general, the length of the antenna (in feet) is equal to the wavelength specified in the table. However, because the wavelength is closely related to the balance and direction of the airplane, the length of the antenna should be adjusted at any time with a rotating shaft to cope with all special situations.

Recently, the trend of using dual antennas has become more and more widespread. This type of installation is no different from the previous one. Only a similar antenna is installed on the right side of the fuselage. The length of each line is about 150 feet. The main benefit of using dual antennas is that the fuselage is easy to balance, the driving is not difficult, and the sound reception is also easier.

The Frequency Characteristics of Audio Frequency Amplifiers 171

— Ming Xiang

Audio frequency amplifiers are an indispensable main component of any radio receiver. Because their input frequency is within the audio range, there is no need for tuning. Therefore, it seems unnecessary to consider their frequency characteristics during design. However, general audio frequency amplifiers cannot equally amplify all high and low audio frequencies. This is especially true for signals above 10,000 Hz, and this point is closely related to the issue of distortion, which cannot be ignored. To avoid this drawback, the following three points should be noted when designing audio frequency amplifiers:

First, it is necessary to maintain equal amplification power for each frequency. The amplification power obtained at each stage should be slightly sacrificed. Although overloaded vacuum tubes can provide strong output, they cannot achieve balanced amplification. To achieve this, the load resistance of the vacuum tube should be chosen to be smaller.

Second, audio frequency amplification vacuum tubes should be selected to have a smaller input resistance. Almost all triodes are suitable for this condition, such as 201A, 37, 56, etc. No. 30 is particularly suitable. This point can increase the amplification power of low frequencies.

Third, regarding the choice of coupling method. Transformer and impedance coupling can easily hinder the uniformity of amplification power due to the influence of inductance. Direct coupling often suffers from instability after prolonged use, which is also not very satisfactory. It is best to adopt the common resistance coupling method.

In addition to the above three points, there are several more methods to adjust or increase the amplification power of various frequencies:

A parallel LC circuit can be added to the plate circuit of the amplification tube (as shown in Figure A). If the amplification power of a certain frequency is low, the LC circuit can be adjusted to resonate with this frequency. At this time, the impedance of the LC circuit is the highest for the resonant frequency, and the voltage drop across L is also the largest. This voltage drop will be added to the voltage drop across the plate resistance, so as to obtain an increase in volume.

Another method to increase the volume of the amplifier is to utilize regeneration (see Figure B). Capacitor C is the one that generates regeneration. Only a very small capacitance is needed, and a portion of the output power can be fed back to the input circuit through this. However, it is necessary to pay attention that the feedback power should not be too strong, causing the vacuum tube to oscillate. The situation is completely the same as using regeneration in the detection stage, which readers can understand.

The grid-plate capacitance of vacuum tubes is extremely unfavorable for high-frequency signals. If it can be leveled off according to the method in Figure C, the volume of high frequencies can be increased.

To increase the volume of low frequencies, the impedance of the signal returning to ground must be reduced to a very low level. This can be achieved by adding a bypass capacitor C (Figure D).

If an audio frequency amplifier can be tested one by one according to the above points, then regardless of the frequency, the maximum equal amplification power can be obtained, and the working efficiency can naturally be better than usual.

The Method of "Soldering" 172

— Yong Yan

To have a good performing radio, the first thing to do is to ensure that the connections in the machine are well connected, so that the current can flow smoothly without obstruction, and then the whole machine can work normally. "Soldering" is the only way to make the wiring connections good. The method is also very simple, but it also requires considerable tools and techniques, otherwise it is difficult to obtain satisfactory results. Now briefly describe the soldering method as follows for reference.

Before soldering, first gather the tools in one place. Including soldering iron, flux, solder, and heating equipment. Soldering irons are also sold in radio parts stores. The copper tip should be selected to be larger (weighing 40 or 50 grams is most suitable), because smaller ones are easily cooled after heating, and there is the trouble of frequent heating; if there is an electric soldering iron, it is more convenient to use. Flux is used to remove oxides on the surface of the metal to be soldered, such as rosin, borax, hydrochloric acid, sodium borate, zinc chloride, etc. Rosin should be used here because it is cheap, easy to obtain, and non-corrosive. Solder is a kind of easily fusible tin alloy, which is sold in Chinese copper and tin shops, commonly known as "hook light". The heating equipment is most convenient with a large alcohol lamp, and a charcoal stove can also be used; but a coal stove is not suitable, because the sulfur in the coal is easy to combine with the copper tip of the soldering iron to form copper sulfide, which hinders soldering; if an electric soldering iron is used, the current heats it.

When everything is ready, make the soldering iron "tinned" (a soldering iron that has not been tinned cannot adhere solder to it). First polish the tip of the soldering iron, then fully heat it to a dull red, and melt a little rosin on it, then apply solder to its tip, so that there is a thin layer of shiny tin.

When soldering, first polish the soldering area to make it shine with metallic luster, then find a way to twist it together, and place a small piece of rosin on it. Then, use the tinned soldering iron to melt an appropriate amount of solder, and make this solder fully distributed on the area to be soldered, and wait for it to cool and solidify to form.

There are several points to pay attention to when working. A. Do not excessively heat the soldering iron, otherwise the tin on its tip will disappear due to overheating, so that it cannot adhere to the solder in the future. (If it can no longer adhere to the solder, it should be "tinned" to remedy it.) Therefore, heat to the degree that it can melt the solder (when green flames occur next to the copper tip of the soldering iron, it means that the heating is sufficient). B. During soldering, the temperature of the area to be soldered must be at the melting point of the solder, otherwise it cannot be soldered firmly. C. This method is suitable for soldering copper, brass, iron, tin, lead, zinc and other metals, but not suitable for soldering aluminum.

The soldering method is very simple, and if you can practice a little, you will be able to handle it with ease.

Shanghai Time for Receiving Short Waves 173

— Zheng Xiyuan

Since shortwave radios have become popular, there are quite a few amateurs who build their own shortwave sets. However, listening to shortwave broadcasts is not as convenient as listening to regular broadcasts. One has to search for broadcast times in foreign shortwave magazines and go through the cumbersome procedures of checking longitudes and latitudes and calculating time differences from maps. The time table below, which has recently been updated, was seen in a Western newspaper. I thought this would be somewhat useful for comrades who love shortwave broadcasts. So I immediately copied and translated it. Although there are only fifteen shortwave broadcasting stations in it, they are all very famous major stations in Europe and Australia. If you have a small shortwave receiver that uses two 30 tubes, as long as the coil matching is accurate and you have a good antenna and ground wire, you can listen to them one by one on time.

Radio Broadcasting in Japan (Continued) 176

— Cai Guanghua

Time and Programs

The broadcasting time is from 6:00 AM to 10:00 PM. The content of the programs includes government bulletins, weather forecasts, education, entertainment, children's time, etc. The time and programs are all formulated by the association by hiring various experts and organizing a broadcasting review committee. In the past two years, the association has solicited opinions from listeners several times on what kind of programs they need. Newspapers also devote a lot of space every day to publish and discuss the programs of the day. Therefore, Japanese people themselves feel that the broadcasting programs in recent years have made significant progress, not only in terms of quantity, but also in terms of quality.

The morning exercises under the leadership of the broadcasting station are worth mentioning. This kind of program has invisibly become a national health movement. When the second summer radio gymnastics was held in August 1933, more than 3,580,000 people participated for about twenty days.

In order to enable listeners in various places to fully understand the language of the reporters (there are also dialects in Japanese, such as the dialects of Tokyo and Kyushu, which are completely different), the association has a movement to standardize the national language, which will definitely make a great contribution to the national language and culture in the future.

As for entertainment, from the aristocratic "Noh drama" to the common people's "Naniwa-bushi" (ancient Japanese drama) in the afternoon, as well as ancient and modern music and old and new folk songs, are constantly being broadcast. The larger radio stations have orchestras, and the regular noon music programs are mostly broadcast by orchestras. At around 8:00 or 9:00 in the evening, it is probably a relay of the song and dance drama from the Takarazuka Girls' Revue Theater, which is the most popular entertainment program.

In terms of education, there are more than a dozen types, including "Adult Education Lectures," "Women's Education Lectures," and "Foreign Language Lectures." What is particularly noteworthy is the "Emergency Lectures." In the past, there were lectures on the Northeast Incident, Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, etc. Now, lectures on World War II and investing in "Manchukuo" are being conducted. Whether it is "Manchuria is Japan's land lifeline" or "The South Pacific Islands are Japan's ocean lifeline," they are constantly giving Japanese citizens a shot in the arm.

Other programs, such as the university league baseball game held every spring and autumn at the Meiji Jingu Stadium in Tokyo, and the national high school league baseball game sponsored by the Asahi Shimbun every summer, are broadcast live by Tokyo JOAK, which is the most popular sports program. (To be continued)

Grains 180

Soybean Oil Import Tax Increase Causes Oil Prices to Soar

A Rise of 7-8 Jiao, Tax of 30%

Yesterday, the miscellaneous grain market suddenly heard that the import tax on soybean oil was increased from the original rate of 15% to 30%. The atmosphere was boiling and indescribable. How to deal with this additional tax on future goods that have always been sold? If the selling firms are responsible, it is said that about 14,000 to 15,000 baskets of soybean oil have been sold, and the tax is levied on each basket of 4.5 dan on the market scale, which is a heavy burden. At this time of extremely tight credit, there is this sudden tax increase. Although the Japanese want to dump Northeast soybean oil and exempt its export tax, each dan is only reduced by about 3 jiao, and the increase is one yuan and several jiao. Therefore, the miscellaneous grain industry sent representatives to the customs to state their opinions, asking them to consider and remedy it from the perspective of people's livelihood and commerce. (According to the regulations, raw materials are still taxed at 15% and have not been increased.) Therefore, people were excited. The market was still flat in the morning, but in the afternoon, the soybean oil market suddenly showed a very abnormal change. Now I have come up with a way for the original envelope workshop to specialize in mounting instead of making, so that the output can be increased by more than double. Our factory cuts the envelope blanks and marks the lines and creases. All you need to do is paste the mouth, and it will be successful. Therefore, even complete amateurs can do it. Taking the tooth powder bag as an example, each person can make 2,000 per day and earn a wage of 4 jiao. Any place can make and sell locally. Today's envelopes mostly need to be printed with advertisements, so for this business, just contact the local printers and supply them with the finished white envelope blanks to print. As long as they are cheap, even cheaper than machine-made envelopes, they are of course welcome to use them, because the labor cost of machine-made envelopes is 4 yuan per 10,000 (excluding mounting labor), so in places where labor is cheap, you can still use handmade to defeat machines. Moreover, because we make our own paper, our purpose is only to promote the sales of paper, so we specially leave this work to be earned by the inland labor force, so that your selling price can still be 1 or 2 yuan cheaper per 10,000 than those machine-made envelopes. The number of sales of printing shops is often 100,000-200,000, and they are definitely taking the cheap route, so you can rest assured about sales. But with a capital of 100-200 yuan, it can become a constant industry. Other things are still afraid of being shelved and never sold. Envelopes are not time-sensitive, so I said that the safest small business industry is nothing more than this. If you want to print red labels yourself, it is also very easy. We have already made a set of simple letterpress printing equipment, arranged the red label version, and equipped it with ink rollers. You can print it yourself, and you can also print business cards. This set of equipment only costs 5 yuan, isn't it extremely cheap?

Free Talk

Children, Lions, Camels 187

— Xiang Yu

I also want to preach like Nietzsche, but my opinion is completely opposite to Nietzsche's. Nietzsche said: "The three metamorphoses of the spirit I designate to you: how the spirit becomes a camel, the camel a lion, and finally the lion a child" (see the English translation of Thus Spoke Zarathustra in the Modern Library); but I believe that if the three metamorphoses of the spirit are natural developments, it is a child transforming into a lion, and a lion transforming into a camel. Due to the different starting points, the difference in opinions is naturally very large, because Nietzsche advocates the superman, but his so-called superman cannot be found in our society. Therefore, the camel that he speaks of bearing heavy burdens must be transformed into a lion, the master of the wilderness, once it reaches the wilderness. And because lions cannot create new values in the wilderness, lions must also become innocent, forgetful, and extremely affirmative children - his superman worldview fundamentally exists outside of reality and is not what I understand. And we advocate ordinary people, which is a fact, not an ideal. In fact, there is no need for any subjective advocacy. In any society, these ordinary people are encountered everywhere, and everyone is one of the ordinary people. With all five senses and all parts of the body, there is nothing missing and nothing extra, which is the standard ordinary person. Occasionally there are one or two people who have some special features that others do not have, but even if there are some special features, they are not characteristics of the superman. If there are, in the society of ordinary people, this is probably not something to be proud of, but rather something to be ridiculed.

Therefore, in the society of ordinary people, supermen cannot be found, and the existence of supermen is not allowed at all. A child is born, and you will see his parents teach him how to become an ordinary person, his teachers teach him how to become an ordinary person; his society teaches him how to become an ordinary person: he is innocent, but his parents, teachers, and society want to teach him to be sensible, and what is called being sensible is naturally to understand the things of ordinary people: he is forgetful, but his parents, teachers, and society want to teach him not to forget, and what is called not forgetting is naturally not to forget the things of ordinary people: he is extremely affirmative, but his parents, teachers, and society want to teach him what you should do (Thou Shall) and what you are not allowed to do (Thou Shall nat). What is called what you should do and what you should not do is naturally to teach him to do things that ordinary people are allowed to do and not to do things that ordinary people are not allowed to do (this was started in the Ten Commandments of Moses "The Commandments" three thousand four hundred years ago). By the time the child becomes an adult, his body, though as strong as a lion, and his character, though still with the wildness of a lion, he is a domesticated member of society, and by no means the master of the wilderness. He is a lion confined in a cage by society! When he gets older, what his eyes see are the things of ordinary people; what his ears hear are the things of ordinary people; what his nose smells is the smell of ordinary people; what he thinks in his heart are the concepts of ordinary people; plus the traditions of the past thousands of years, the social customs that cannot be liquidated at present, he is a complete camel bearing heavy burdens.

I believe that in the society of ordinary people, the transformation of the spirit is a child transforming into a lion, and a lion transforming into a camel.

Another Discussion of "One Method Leads to All" 188

— Chen Zizhan

Wu Xie's "One Method Leads to All" was recently sent to me by Mr. Lu Dubu of Yuezhou. This book by the elder Mr. Wu is truly very interesting. At the beginning of the book is his preface, written in "the seventh month of the Yi Si year of Guangxu," and the title page states "engraved in the Bing Wu year of Guangxu," which, calculating it, is just about thirty years ago.

Why did he write this book?

Originally, he wanted to use it to replace elementary textbooks. At that time, the elementary textbooks used in new schools roughly started with recognizing characters and then explaining them. The characters were concrete words, also called static words. After accumulating dozens of characters, they would then learn to fill in words and piece together sentences. This was certainly an improvement over the old method of memorizing the Four Books and Five Classics in private schools. However, the elder Mr. Wu still felt that this method was not enough, believing that single characters were difficult to remember, and it would be better to recognize and explain characters while simultaneously teaching and piecing together sentences. Moreover, concrete and abstract words should be taught together, so why distinguish them? Therefore, he wanted to write "One Method Leads to All." In my opinion, it is indeed ten times better than elementary textbooks of the time, such as "Character Lessons with Illustrations." Unfortunately, I didn't get this book when I was first learning, otherwise, I might have suffered less in my language learning.

Can this book actually be used to teach beginners?

According to the elder Mr. Wu's own experience, he said:

"If children in my family study the classics for three years and still don't understand, they will all understand after studying this for one year. Those who cannot write family letters will all be able to."

This is certainly reliable. Think about it, how can you explain the great way of the sages in the classics to children? It's useless even if you explain it for three years. "One Method Leads to All" is a rhyming book compiled with proverbs, which is easy to read aloud, easy to explain clearly, and easy to remember. Of course, after reading and explaining it, they will understand in one year and be able to write family letters. The elder Mr. Wu did not belittle the classics, nor did he rebel against the way of the sages. However, for the sake of children's learning and happiness, he did not advocate reading and explaining the classics. He had a considerable understanding of the elementary textbooks of the new schools at that time, and he even took the initiative to compile a proverb reader. An old gentleman thirty years ago had this insight, which truly makes us unenterprising younger generations ashamed to death!

This book is compiled according to the order of rhyme categories, a total of three volumes, bound in three books. Now, I will excerpt a little bit from the last article of the last volume, the "Moon" rhyme, to give a glimpse of the book's content.

The boat can pass, the rudder can pass. I can report the tune, but I cannot sing it.

If it doesn't blow, it's still cold. If you don't owe debts, you can still be poor.

The main house is extinct, the side house prospers. The upper house is uncle, the lower house is cousin.

Measles must be vented, smallpox must scab. Wrap everything, sweep everything.

The clan has merit, the ancestors have virtue. The north goes to the Xiongnu, the south goes to the Yue.

Not afraid of nonsense, but afraid of no speech.

Grain is collected in August, money is collected in December.

Better to be hit by a mountain man, than by a water man.

Hitting gold, you recognize gold, hitting iron, you recognize iron.

A thousand murderers, eight hundred aggrieved.

To have such a virtuous host, and not have such a bad guest.

Tattered clothes harbor lice, dilapidated houses harbor thieves.

Killing people, you see blood, saving people, you save thoroughly.

Marry a wife for virtue, marry a concubine for beauty.

Though father and son are close, their financial minds are different.

If you know how to litigate, only litigate halfway.

Painting water, you paint sound, painting fire, you paint heat.

Each scholar has his own ambition, why force each other?

Taking risks, how can you choose in a hurry?

Borrow a thousand, don't need to pay back eight hundred right now.

What's real cannot be faked, what's fake cannot be real.

Hundred goods, hundred customers, cotton, cotton fluff customers.

Enter the door, observe the face, leave the door, observe the sky.

Words on the wall are hard to stick, words on the mat are hard to say.

Big business fears losses, small business fears shutting down.

Chess is the barren field board, cards are the field-selling book.

Saying words, eyes rolling white, this person cannot be associated with.

A little secret in the world, don't tell your wife and children.

The blacksmith doesn't drop iron, but pinches a piece right in front of you.

Selling soy milk and encountering cold weather, selling meat and encountering hot weather.

A medical family will surely prosper for three generations, a medical family will surely be wiped out for three generations.

When inviting guests, don't invite female guests, invite fifty, and a hundred will come.

Stewing loach in a stove, eat one piece, stew one piece.

Starting a family is like picking up with a needle, ruining a family is like snow melting in hot water.

From the top of the head, the Niwan Palace, to the soles of the feet, the Yongquan acupoint.

A monkey picks up a piece of ginger, can't eat it, can't throw it away.

The public repairs, the public gets, the old woman repairs, the old woman gets. Each repairs, each gets, if you don't repair, you won't get.

The above words are all popular slang in Hunan folk now, of course, many of them are common to various places. These living languages ​​can be used as rhetoric in vernacular writing. Don't say that the vocabulary of vernacular language is poor, and you have to go to classical books to find it. In my humble opinion, this book can be called "Proverb Reader." If someone compiles proverbs from various places, and uses Mr. Wu's method of dividing rhymes to compile a "Dictionary of Popular Rhymes" for general new writers to use to pick up rhetoric, so as to avoid going to ancient books and going astray, it would be truly a great merit!

Life 189

— Translated by Bilan Terrace Luo Zuofengzi

Let the delicate wisps of smoke,

Twine around my mind of illusion;

Look at the vast sky,

Enveloping the owls on the ground.

Where is the lodging of the heart,

What is the joy of life?

Let me chew on the bitter cigarette butt,

Gazing blankly at the boundless horizon.

Small Roadside Shop (Part Two) 190

— Liu Ming

The person whose ear was pulled, smiled mockingly while touching their reddened ear.

At first, I only felt a little surprised, but now, I was also made to laugh by this sentence, because judging from the hostess's wrinkled face and the fact that two or three teeth had fallen out, her true age seemed to be right for reversing fifteen years, and saying she was fifty.

"How could I be like fifteen years old!" She said, carrying the two umbrellas to the door and shaking off the water droplets on them, distractedly, while sighing as if suddenly realizing something, "At that time, who didn't mistake me for Miss Li's family? Alas, the clothes and accessories I wore..." Her gaze shot towards the Baiyi village and the late spring fields mixed with misty rain across the road, and she was silent for a while.

Probably my three companions were already familiar with her background, and they were not interested in asking about the story hidden in this sentence, but they joked even more interestingly.

"Hehe, why did you abandon being a young lady? Now, you've only ended up... Who is to blame..."

The private cigarette peddler actually sang mockingly in the Beijing opera tune he had heard from the city, but he swallowed the too lewd words in his throat and did not spit them out.

She immediately realized that she was being mocked, and immediately turned around, waved the umbrella near the private cigarette peddler, hit the empty space, and asked back with a stern face as if scolding:

"If that tigress hadn't branded people's backs with a soldering iron, who would be willing to run to Yifang Dam?"

Probably because I was a stranger, she glanced at me uneasily, and then pursed her wrinkled thin lips at the private cigarette peddler.

"If it were you, you would have died in that den long ago!"

When she said this, her tone seemed to be full of pride and glory. The private cigarette peddler didn't answer, just wiped the water droplets sprinkled on his face, and scolded:

"Damn it, drop your umbrella!"

At this time, the Baiyi monk seemed to have taken two or three pleasant puffs of smoke and enjoyed himself a little, so he sat up, re-draped the robe that had been scattered by sleep over his shoulder, and greeted the man who was cooking the opium happily.

"Zhe Nong, is it ready yet?"

She hurried over and carefully responded.

"Does the Buddha want another box?"

After the Baiyi monk left, she lay down, grabbed the opium pipe, and shouted softly and charmingly to the man cooking the opium:

"Come and lie down for a while, I'll burn you a good bubble!"

The sedan chair carrier put his arm around the person beside him and whispered with winking eyes:

"Look how affectionate they are!"

The private cigarette peddler, however, returned to his normal state, yawned, and said with a flat mouth:

"Bah, an old sow!"

At this moment, I suddenly understood why they had burst into laughter at my words just now, but a vein of mysterious mist hung in my heart as if enveloping the rain and smoke in the other side of the Baiyi.

The man did not go to bed to smoke opium, and he did not seem to agree, but showed his sturdy back in the thick rising steam.

The old hostess angrily threw the opium pipe into the wooden plate, sighed, and fell asleep silently.

We all stopped talking and turned our bored eyes to the outside of the door. The woods and thatched houses shrouded in misty rain sometimes appeared vaguely and sometimes disappeared, turning into a single color of heaven and earth, but the raindrops on the eaves kept ringing without stopping.

Good News 191

— TK

Reply to "Between Tears and Laughter" 192

— Qian Di

I didn't expect that "The Malaysian of Eggplant Banana" in Free Talk could arouse Mr. Shao Yin's "Between Tears and Laughter," which makes me feel so honored!

However, it is a pity that Mr. Shao Yin's vision only likes to look at the big things, but doesn't like to look at the small ones, which makes Mr. Shao Yin fall into the cage of error and "Between Tears and Laughter"!

Mr. Shao Yin thought that what I said in Free Talk about the great assimilation power of the Chinese was only based on the small matter of gambling, and I didn't say "how big is it to give us proof," so he "dared not believe that the Chinese have the ability to assimilate Malaysians." From this, it can be fully seen that Mr. Shao Yin's vision only likes to look at the big things, but doesn't like to look at the small ones, because gambling is a small thing.

However, when we observe a certain thing, we must understand its authenticity from its most subtle aspects. If we only like to observe its large parts or its external form, we will often make mistakes in our understanding. There are naturally many examples of Chinese people assimilating Malays in Southeast Asia, and the reason why I only cited gambling as an example is that I believe that gambling is the easiest thing to flow into the lower class society and make people obsessed. Chinese people and Malaysians are two ethnic groups with different languages, scripts, customs, and habits. It is definitely not possible to assimilate these two completely different ethnic groups into one ethnic group in just ten, twenty years, or hundreds of years. It is not like two piles of clay that can be immediately kneaded into an idol at will. It must go through a long period of assimilation to be completed. Therefore, when two ethnic groups begin to assimilate, it must start from the smallest events in daily life. Although the smallest events are not limited to gambling, gambling is one of the smallest events in daily life. Can we deny that the Malaysians of eggplant banana have not been assimilated by the Chinese in their thinking about gambling? If the Malaysians of eggplant banana did not have the political protection of the British, who knows if they would not be completely assimilated by the Chinese in a hundred years or so?

Carefully examining Mr. Shao Yin's meaning, he thought that my citing gambling as an example was too small. Okay, let me give Mr. Shao Yin one or two larger examples. But to what extent they are large, I don't know, I have to ask Mr. Shao Yin to measure it himself.

First, in the South Seas Islands, there is a small island, Portuguese territory, called Timor (also known as Moore), where Chinese copper coins are used, Chinese language is spoken, and customs and habits are completely old forms brought from China. It is impossible for the Malaysians there not to want to assimilate with the Chinese.

Second, in a small mountain port in Belitung, Dutch East Indies (I can't remember the place name for a while), not only Chinese language is popular among the people, but also Chinese language is used in the court.

From these two points, Mr. Shao Yin will not have "dare not believe that the Chinese have the ability to assimilate Malaysians" again. In fact, the current Malaysians in the British and Dutch colonies can maintain their temporary survival only because of the political protection of the British and Dutch imperialism. Otherwise, I am afraid they would have been eliminated long ago.

Finally, what I want to say is that the main reason for the British's active anti-Chinese in recent years is naturally the serious aggravation of the economic panic. However, the gradual assimilation of Malaysians by the Chinese is also one of the reasons for promoting their anti-Chinese. The anti-Chinese in South Africa, Mexico, San Francisco, and the Dutch East Indies before the European War was not for economic panic at all, because capitalism was still in its golden age at that time. At that time, their anti-Chinese was because the Chinese everywhere took the place of the indigenous people with their spirit of perseverance and hard work, which made the imperialists feel chills.

The Cripple (Part Three) 193

— (Written by Zsigmond Moricz) Translated by Uncle Zhuang

"How do you five sleep in this room?"

"Very comfortably, my husband takes one of the three children to sleep on the bed, and I, with the other two children, sleep on a bundle of wheat straw on the ground."

"Even in winter?"

"Of course. Ah! This is a very good little house, as warm as a stove."

So, proudly, she showed me everything she had; a salt jar placed on a shelf, a flour box placed under the bed, a small kerosene lamp placed on the table. I have never seen a housewife more proud of her housework than she.

I continued to talk to her. She answered my questions with an intelligent frankness and a clear, cheerful voice.

"How did you meet your husband?" I asked her.

"Ah! This is a very strange thing, a true novel... At first, people praised him to me, people told me that a cripple was very suitable to be matched with me. Then, he doesn't drink, he's not vulgar, and he also has a good lifelong allowance... I, I lived in a neighboring village, my husband died in the war, and I thought, 'I should go see him, or this is God's will...' So, you know, he immediately loved me, because this is a very sincere man.

Did he use a flower car to greet you according to the customs here? Did your master use a four-horse carriage to pick you up here?"

"Ah! You think!" the woman said, "People were immediately jealous of my luck, and wanted to take him away from me. I should tell you that people said many rumors about me, saying that I was too fond of dressing up, and not worthy of being a poor man's wife."

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Germany Again Becomes the Hammer of the World 194

— Qing

Germany was once a country that wanted to be the "hammer of the world." Before the war, it had the ambition to monopolize Europe and even the world. But since being defeated by Britain, France and other countries in 1917, this ambition has been wiped out.

Since then, Germany has completely become a "anvil of the world," severely hammered by major powers—especially France.

And now, a few ambitious people in Germany have the ambition to become the "hammer of the world" again. According to reports, German Labor Administrator Boerge said in a speech to the National Socialist Party youth in Cologne: "Germany will no longer be the anvil of the world in the future, but will be the hammer of the world." What an exaggerated tone.

In fact, Germany's desire to become the hammer of the world again did not start today. Since Hitler came to power, he has even more enthusiastically stirred up this ambition. However, the result of his efforts is to demand equality in armaments and to demand the return of the Saar region, etc., which have all been severely repulsed by Britain and France. Germany had no choice, so it could only withdraw from the League of Nations, simply close the door, and simply manufacture the hammer of the world.

If Germany wants to become the hammer of the world again, naturally, the first thing it must do is to hammer down its only target enemy, France. However, this is what Britain seems not to fully allow. Moreover, with France's current strength, it is difficult for Germany to have the power to hammer it down. Then, where will its iron hammer go? It's towards Russia, which has a vast territory. Therefore, the only person it can hammer at the moment is Russia. This is why today's Germany has become the only factor in Western Europe that can trigger a world war.

Similarly, Japan in the East is also fully and sweetly dreaming of becoming the "hammer of the world." This dream can be said to be half realized for it. Now the problem is Russia. How will Japan's "hammer of the world" strike into Russian territory? This is very hesitant. Furthermore, the United States on the east coast is also its mortal enemy. As long as these two enemies are not a problem, its "hammer of the world" dream seems to be 80 or 90 percent complete.

However, this dream will probably never be completed. Let's see how it is triumphant in its dreams and how it is frustrated in its dreams.

After Illness 195

— Chang Er

After being sick, I supported myself with a cane and took a walk alone in the park.

It was winter, quiet and silent. The path lay before me like an abandoned woman. The small trees on both sides rustled in the wind. Occasionally, a few yellow leaves rolled a few times over my head and fell into the muddy ground.

Looking up, I couldn't see the dense shade of the sky in winter, only a few thin tree trunks. The sun didn't feel warm on my body at all. This park also seemed to be sick and lifeless.

"A sympathetic child is here to see you!"

Whistling, I sat down on an empty iron sand chair, took out a book of poems from my coat, which a friend who didn't sign his name had sent to me from the post office when I was sick. On the cover were two lines of delicate handwriting:

Knowing that you are sick, I am sending you this book of poems as a pastime during your illness. Don't pursue the person who sent the book, we will have a chance to meet.

I flipped through it casually every day, and after reading each poem, it seemed that I had seen it somewhere, but there was no author's name or publishing house at the bottom of the page. It wasn't because of the suggestion in those two lines that I didn't try to think about who sent the book. I really didn't have that kind of thought during my illness. After reading it, I just piled it on the bookshelf. Later, after I moved, I didn't know where this book of poems was stuck. Today, while sorting out my clothes, I found it at the bottom of a broken box and stuffed it in my big night bag. Now that I saw those two lines again, I wanted to pursue the person who sent the book.

I stared at a group of sparrows foraging for food on the ground, and my thoughts followed their jumps, not knowing where they had gone. Suddenly, they flew away together, and a figure flashed at the end of the path.

"Another sympathetic child is here!"

Thinking, I watched a pair of high-heeled leather shoes slowly walk over from the withered yellow grass. My eyes lifted from her toes, and I quickly buried my head in my collar as if reading a book, listening quietly to the sound of the footsteps getting closer and closer. The toes had stopped in front of me. At the same time, someone patted me on the shoulder. I pretended to be suddenly startled and looked up.

"You've lost weight—I still recognize you."

"Yes, I've been sick for a long time."

I stood up and stuffed the book of poems into my coat pocket, wanting to walk away.

"I know," she supported my cane and walked side by side. "I wanted to visit you, but you moved."

I glanced at her, thought of the book of poems, and waved it in front of her.

"Did you send it?"

Nodding, "These are the poems you like to read."

"But the second time is not as interesting as the first time!"

"Then maybe you are not satisfied with the person who writes the poems?"

"I don't mean that, I am satisfied with every poet... Poets are passionate, aren't they?"

"Poor mouth!" Smiling, she kicked a small brick on the road, "Don't remember the past, poets are as free as the white clouds in the sky."

"Congratulations on being able to publish your second book of poems!"

"Seriously, can you tell me your address?"

"Are you planning to send me a book of poems? Thank you, my bookshelf is already full!"

"Okay, I live in a women's apartment, I hope

Page 21

we will have a chance to meet again!"

I watched her disappear into the side of the road, stepping on the yellow leaves. I looked up, and the white clouds were flying in the sky.

"Free!" I stared again at the two lines of delicate handwriting on the cover.

The City God Temple and the Great World 196

— Wu Shi

When foreigners come to China to sightsee, when they step on the land of Shanghai, the place names they can call out are the City God Temple and the Great World, as if these two places can represent the entire metropolis of Shanghai. Every tourist group that comes to Shanghai often finds a string of cars or rickshaws in these two places. As a result, many untrue news and photos are taken back to their countries for dishonest publicity. Foreign writers who create behind closed doors think that the whole of China is like this. This is still the case in Shanghai, the largest metropolis in the East. If they go deep into the culturally backward inland and feudal small villages, when they mention China, they can use braids and foot binding to represent it, which is not an exaggeration.

The conversation has gone so far, but in fact, the City God Temple and the Great World are just like Nanjing Road and the Great Light in the minds of people. Isn't it crowded with people every day?

When I was a child, I went to the City God Temple with my grandfather every day. In the eyes of a child, it was probably better than a tour group. The stalls selling sugar and various toys were all considered wonders of the world. Even watching the turtles crawling up with their heads raised on the Zigzag Bridge was particularly exciting. But when my grandfather arrived at the temple, he would go to the tea house. He never allowed me to run around, saying that I would be caught by kidnappers. So, I was satisfied with the small-scale overlooking of the patterns on the foreign railings. However, what gave me the impression of the City God Temple was not these, but the small stalls selling peanuts and dried tofu. Because the guests in this tea house were all my grandfather's friends, and when they met, they could talk a lot. When they talked, they naturally couldn't spare the energy to take care of me. Afraid that I would sneak down to play, they would reward the three armies and grab a table of snacks. So, the impression the City God Temple gave me was not fun, but delicious. Now it is said that the City God Temple still prevails in the "eat" aspect. From the front door, there are chestnut stalls, open-air dishes, noodle shops with meat and vegetables, and various snacks. It's simply a stall every five steps and a shop every ten steps. However, if you want me to find what foreigners think is unique, I am afraid it is those statues. However, compared with "God," there is not much difference.

Speaking of the Great World, I am really sorry. If it weren't for the diving friends showing their skills this summer, I wouldn't have had anything to do with it. So, what the Great World was like before, I can't imagine. However, the game venue is always a collection of miscellaneous things, and the tickets must be cheap. It is the only place for the so-called country people to come to Shanghai, as well as many shop assistants and workers, to have fun. People from other places can watch their local operas, which is of course particularly cordial. Beijing opera and spoken drama also have their supporters. I spent three hours making a patrol, and in addition to the fact that the crowds here were too disorderly, I also couldn't find anything that the foreign adults thought was particularly worthy of. I spent three yuan to watch the Kaleidoscope Troupe. I forgot that the clowns in one of the scenes were rolling all over the stage. What is the difference between this and the Great Brook Royal Estate here?

The City God Temple and the Great World have their own value and history. This point may be what the tour group pays special attention to.

A Word From Life's Treasure Chest 197

— Gote

—A Thousand Sensations—

In the eyes of a pauper, this world is no different from a volcano, just like hell.

In the mouth of a tycoon, this world is the most blissful, as if it were heaven.

Only women understand true sorrow, only children know nothing of worldly worries, and only the elderly understand the true hardships of life. Only religious figures thoroughly understand the mystery of women, and only revolutionaries understand the fate of the world.

Life is meaningful when one is successful, and tasteless when one is frustrated.

Those who fear life are troubled by it, those who love life are trapped by it, those who do not understand life are harmed by it, and those who understand life are loved by it.

Those who wear tinted glasses see everything in color. Conversely, they are often dazzled by the colorful world.

I want to hold the world in my own palm. But the world kneads me under its armpit.

I want to make all the women in the world my slaves, but I am treated as their slave by all the women in the world.

I think that if people were not living for life, they would not fight each other.

If you are not selfish, I am not self-interested, and he is not self-loving, then everyone will be happy.

I think that the heads of foreigners are made of machines, the mouths of women are made of honey, the hearts of Chinese people are tofu-shaped, the feet of soldiers are cast in iron, and the hands of warlords are crab claws.

I hate those who love me. I love those who hate me.

Those without cultivation love noise, and those with learning prefer silence.

Those with narrow minds will never succeed in life.

Struggle is the driving force for the success of all undertakings.

Those with unwavering will will not fail; because they will not be discouraged by failure.

The most foolish people are the happiest people.

There is no one who does not lie, and no one who lies all their life.

Those who like to sneer are cunning. Those who are cunning are good at harming others.

Those who treat others with sincerity are often deceived by those who are not sincere.

Humans are the most intelligent of all things, but also the culprit of all things, because humans only care about humans.

The Master's Favor 198

— Da Ye

The little maid, Xiangxiang, stood in the corner by the door, watching Madam.

Madam, in front of the dressing table, applied powder, drew her eyebrows, shaded her eye circles, put on rouge, dabbed lipstick, all the way from head to toe.

Facing the mirror, Madam put on makeup for a long time, imitating the expressions she learned from the movies: smiling, acting coy.

Her large eyes in the mirror drifted to the young man standing next to her; the young man smiled, a smile that was somewhat impatient from waiting too long.

"Am I ready? Am I pretty enough!"

"Alright, don't rush."

Madam stood up giggling, turned to look at her back, then went to the coat rack to get her coat. The young man eagerly stepped forward to help her put it on.

Holding her arm, Madam sent a kiss to her husband, who was sitting alone at the table sipping beer, and then, in a coquettish voice, said, "Goodbye!" and swayed her hips out.

Xiangxiang paid attention to the husband's expression after Madam left, but he did not look angry, sipping his wine with a smug look.

Suddenly, the husband raised his voice and shouted, "Xiangxiang!"

As usual, after hearing this call, Xiangxiang brought up the prepared milk coffee.

As always, the husband smiled at her behind Madam's back, squinting his eyes and smiling: "Xiangxiang, you work so hard every day cooking, I feel very sorry."

Very restrained, she said, "It's no hardship, it's my duty to earn the Master's money and cook."

At this moment, the husband suddenly took out five yuan and said, "You are very diligent, I will pay you your salary for next month in advance."

"Thank you, Master."

Unexpectedly, the husband reached out and pulled her to his side, saying he had something to say to her, and whispered in her ear for a while. Her face flushed, and she just shook her head, pulling her hand away.

The husband still grinned and said to her, "Why are you such a silly girl? It's because the Master sees you in a good light that he wants to favor you. To be honest, Madam is very wealthy and carefree now, but wasn't she the same as you before? After she married me, I often took her out for social gatherings, and that's how she became wealthy. Now who would see her as a maid? You should think about it!"

Xiangxiang remained silent. The husband made a face and walked up to her, "If you agree to me, won't you have more than enough to enjoy when I dump Madam?"

Thinking of home, thinking of herself, thinking of the husband's words, thinking that if she agreed to the husband, wouldn't he abandon her just like he abandoned Madam? She was so scared that she trembled all over.

Xiangxiang trembled and said, "Master, I can't, I can't..."

"You should think about it, you'll never get ahead if you're a servant all your life. If you agree to me, will you still have to worry about food and clothing?"

Xiangxiang shook her head.

The husband became a little angry, "If you continue to be so unappreciative, don't make me angry. Tell me, are you willing or not?"

Still shaking her head.

The husband stood up angrily and snatched the money from Xiangxiang's hand.

"Get out!"

"Get out of what?"

Xiangxiang was stunned?

Farewell Shanghai 199

— Ah Jiong

Around noon, clouds floated in the sky, with patches of black emerging, and a thin mist covered the ground. It was like the scene of deep autumn, with fine rain falling incessantly, and with the mist, it gradually felt thicker. In such a scene, I entrusted myself to the huge ship, leaving my F, arriving in Shanghai.

Because F was waiting for me at the pier, and the time for the ship to depart was very tight, I braved the rain and came out of the house with a heart as miserable as when I left home for the first time. The scenes on the street were still the same as usual: crowds of people coming and going, cars weaving back and forth, trams still running at full speed, dragging forward like long snakes. The autumn wind blew the fallen leaves on the ground, and the autumn rain continued to fall gently, as unpleasant as the plum rain. I followed the rotation of the wheels listlessly and arrived at the Bund wharf, where I and the dock worker carrying F's luggage boarded the ship.

Looking at the vast sea, all was boundless. Where would this small boat carry me? I carried a heavy burden on my back. Would this burden be battered by several storms and not sink to the bottom of the sea? I began to feel apprehensive, and my heart trembled uncontrollably. F held my hand tightly, and there seemed to be unspeakable pain between us, at the moment when this separation was about to come. The whip of life is so harsh! In order to survive, I had to separate from F and drift alone to the strange southern country.

In the sound of the whistle, F stood from the deck to the dock. The gong rang, and the ship seemed to start to turn. Oh, my heart! It was simply too painful to describe! I don't know why, but a feeling of sadness, that it is easy to part but difficult to meet again, surged from the depths of my heart like a tide. I had no power to stop it at all, and I finally cried!

The ship sailed, and in the bleak autumn wind and the misty rain, F's figure standing on the dock finally became too small to see clearly. I said sadly to the sea and sky: Farewell, farewell, Shanghai!

Opening Chapter "Zhu Maichen Divorces His Wife"

Chinese Classics 204

Ms. Bingmei's Tang Poetry

Huaxing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Mountain Rock

The mountain rocks are uneven, and the path is narrow and winding. At dusk, bats fly to the temple.

Climbing the hall and sitting on the steps, the new rain is abundant. The banana leaves are large, and the gardenia is fertile.

The monk said that the ancient wall had good Buddhist paintings. He lit a fire to see what was rarely seen.

Spreading the bed and dusting the mat, setting out soup and rice. Coarse grains are enough to satisfy my hunger.

Deep in the night, lying quietly, all insects are gone. The clear moon rises from the ridge, and light enters the door.

At dawn, I leave alone, with no road. Going in and out, high and low, into the misty rain.

The mountains are red, the streams are blue, and the poplar and elm are lush and abundant. Sometimes I see pines and elms all ten spans around.

Stepping on the stream stones with bare feet, the sound of the water is激激, and the wind rises on my clothes.

Life is so pleasant, why must I be constrained and ridiculed by others?

Alas, my party of two or three friends, how can we not return until old age?

Gifting Zhang Gongcao on the Night of the Fifteenth of August

Weaving clouds, four volumes, the sky has no river. The clear wind blows through the air, and the moon spreads its waves.

The sand is flat, the water is calm, and sounds and shadows are gone. Raising a cup to each other, you should sing.

Your song is sad, and the words are bitter. I cannot listen to the end, and tears fall like rain.

Dongting connects to the sky, and Jiuyi is high. Dragons and sea monsters appear and disappear, and apes and squirrels howl.

Nine deaths out of ten lead to the official post. Living in seclusion, silently, as if hiding and fleeing.

Getting out of bed, I fear snakes, and eating, I fear medicine. The sea air is humid, and insects hibernate, exuding a fishy and foul smell.

Yesterday, drums were beaten in front of the state office. The heir emperor succeeded to the throne and ascended Kui Gao.

The amnesty decree travels ten thousand miles in a day. Crimes from capital punishment are all pardoned.

Those who were exiled are recalled, and those who fled return. Washing away blemishes and cleansing the dynasty.

The state family submits the name, and the envoy family suppresses it. Unfortunate, I can only move to Jingman.

The judge's official is lowly and unspeakable. I cannot avoid being whipped and covered in dust.

My contemporaries mostly take the path to the top. The road to heaven is secluded and dangerous, and difficult to catch up with.

Stop your song and listen to mine. How am I different from you?

The bright moon is especially plentiful tonight. Life is determined by fate, not by other things.

With wine, why not drink under the bright moon?

The entire "Sister Flowers" broadcast script, compiled by Li Changjian and published by Yuanchang Advertising Company at No. 323, Anna King Road, La Fayette Road, this city, has been popular since its publication. The book has recently been scheduled to be broadcast by the Li Changjian Broadcasting Troupe from 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM every evening at the Yuanchang Radio Station (frequency 1120) affiliated with the company. In order to treat the listeners, Yuanchang Advertising Company has decided to make a big sacrifice this Sunday (i.e. the 25th). All those who purchase a copy of the Sister Flowers book from the company on this day will have a special discount of five corners, and will also receive a set of guest hall couplets written by Mr. Li Changjian. This offer is only valid for one day and will not be offered again the next day. This is a golden opportunity that only comes once in a thousand years, and it is also the goal of Yuanchang Radio to treat the listeners.
